## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 00:48:24)

The user wants to explore an idea about connecting sessions between mimo-platform and mimo-agent through the ACP (Agent Communication Protocol). They're describing a problem where when mimo-agent restarts, the session is lost in mimo-platform even though message history exists. They want both to share the same session ID and for mimo-platform to be able to resume/reload the session when mimo-agent restarts.

Let me first understand the current state of the codebase to see how sessions are currently handled. I should look at:
1. How mimo-platform manages sessions
2. How mimo-agent handles sessions
3. The ACP protocol and how it relates to sessions
4. Any existing session management code

Let me start by exploring the codebase structure to understand the architecture.
## Agent (2026-04-07 00:48:26)

<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/README.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: # MIMO Platform
2: 
3: A minimal, Emacs-style web-based editor for AI-assisted development.
4: 
5: ## Overview
6: 
7: MIMO (Minimal IDE for Modern Operations) is a platform that enables AI-assisted development through a web-based interface with an Emacs-style workflow. It provides session-based development with worktrees, file synchronization, and integrated chat with AI agents.
8: 
9: ## Features
10: 
11: - **Public Landing Page**: View platform overview and public projects without authentication
12: - **Project Descriptions**: Add optional descriptions to projects for better discoverability
13: - **Emacs-Style Interface**: Three-buffer layout with customizable keybindings
14: - **Session-Based Development**: Work with isolated worktrees for each development session
15: - **File Synchronization**: Automatic sync between agent worktree and original repository
16: - **Integrated Chat**: Real-time chat with AI agents via WebSocket
17: - **VCS Integration**: Fossil as intermediary for both Git and Fossil repositories
18: - **Agent Lifecycle**: Spawn and manage AI agents with JWT authentication
19: - **Conflict Detection**: Smart conflict detection with baseline checksums
20: 
21: ## Architecture
22: 
23: ```
24: ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
25: │                      Browser (Client)                       │
26: │  ┌─────────────┐  ┌─────────────┐  ┌─────────────────┐   │
27: │  │ Files Tree  │  │   Chat      │  │    Changes      │   │
28: │  │   (Left)    │  │  (Center)   │  │    (Right)      │   │
29: │  └─────────────┘  └─────────────┘  └─────────────────┘   │
30: └─────────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────┘
31:                           │ WebSocket / HTTP
32: ┌─────────────────────────▼─────────────────────────────────┐
33: │                 mimo-platform (Hono/Bun)                   │
34: │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
35: │  │  Auth  │  Projects  │  Sessions  │  Agents  │ Sync │  │
36: │  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
37: │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
38: │  │              WebSocket Handlers                      │  │
39: │  │         (Chat, Agent Connections)                  │  │
40: │  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
41: └─────────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────┘
42:                           │
43: ┌─────────────────────────▼─────────────────────────────────┐
44: │                   mimo-agent (Binary)                      │
45: │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
46: │  │         File Watcher  │  ACP Process Proxy        │  │
47: │  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
48: └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
49: ```
50: 
51: ## Installation
52: 
53: ### Prerequisites
54: 
55: - [Bun](https://bun.sh) 1.0+
56: - [Fossil](https://fossil-scm.org) 2.27+
57: - Git (for Git repository support)
58: 
59: ### Quick Start
60: 
61: ```bash
62: # Clone the repository
63: git clone https://github.com/your-org/mimo.git
64: cd mimo
65: 
66: # Install dependencies
67: cd packages/mimo-platform
68: bun install
69: 
70: # Start the server
71: bun run dev
72: ```
73: 
74: The platform will be available at `http://localhost:3000`
75: 
76: ### Build the Agent
77: 
78: ```bash
79: cd packages/mimo-agent
80: bun install
81: bun run build
82: ```
83: 
84: This creates `dist/mimo-agent` which is used by the platform.
85: 
86: ## Usage
87: 
88: ### Public Landing Page
89: 
90: When you first navigate to `http://localhost:3000`, you'll see a public landing page displaying:
91: - Platform overview and features
92: - List of all public projects (names, descriptions, owners, repo types)
93: - Login and Register buttons
94: 
95: Clicking on a project card will redirect you to login if not authenticated, or take you directly to the project detail if authenticated.
96: 
97: ### Authentication
98: 
99: 1. Navigate to `http://localhost:3000/auth/register`
100: 2. Create an account
101: 3. Login at `http://localhost:3000/auth/login`
102: 
103: ### Creating a Project
104: 
105: 1. Click "Create Project" on the projects page
106: 2. Enter project name
107: 3. Add an optional description (recommended ~200 chars, max 500)
108: 4. Provide Git or Fossil repository URL
109: 5. The system imports/clones the repository
110: 
111: ### Starting a Session
112: 
113: 1. Select a project from the projects list
114: 2. Click "New Session"
115: 3. Enter session name
116: 4. The system sets up a Fossil worktree
117: 
118: ### Working with Agents
119: 
120: 1. In a session, click "Start Agent"
121: 2. The platform spawns an agent process
122: 3. Chat with the agent in the center buffer
123: 4. File changes appear in the right buffer automatically
124: 
125: ### Committing Changes
126: 
127: 1. Make changes through the agent
128: 2. Click "Commit" button or press `C-x c`
129: 3. Enter commit message
130: 4. Changes are committed to Fossil and pushed to the original repository
131: 
132: ## Configuration
133: 
134: Configuration is stored in `~/.mimo/config.yaml`:
135: 
136: ```yaml
137: theme: dark
138: fontSize: 14
139: fontFamily: monospace
140: keybindings:
141:   cancel_request: "C-c C-c"
142:   commit: "C-x c"
143:   find_file: "C-x C-f"
144:   switch_project: "C-x p"
145:   switch_session: "C-x s"
146:   focus_left: "C-x h"
147:   focus_center: "C-x j"
148:   focus_right: "C-x l"
149: ```
150: 
151: Edit via the web UI at `/config` or directly in the file.
152: 
153: ## Directory Structure
154: 
155: ```
156: ~/.mimo/
157: ├── config.yaml           # User configuration
158: ├── users/
159: │   └── {username}/
160: │       └── credentials.yaml
161: ├── projects/
162: │   └── {project-id}/
163: │       ├── project.yaml
164: │       ├── repo.fossil
165: │       ├── original/     # Original repo worktree
166: │       └── sessions/
167: │           └── {session-id}/
168: │               ├── session.yaml
169: │               ├── chat.jsonl
170: │               ├── repo.fossil       # Fossil proxy for agent sync
171: │               ├── upstream/         # Original repository clone
172: │               └── agent-workspace/  # Agent working directory (plain files)
173: └── agents/
174:     └── {agent-id}/
175:         └── agent.yaml
176: ```
177: 
178: ### Session Directory Structure
179: 
180: Each session directory contains:
181: 
182: - `session.yaml` - Session metadata (name, status, port, agentWorkspacePath, upstreamPath)
183: - `chat.jsonl` - Chat message history
184: - `repo.fossil` - Fossil proxy repository for agent synchronization
185: - `upstream/` - Clone of the original repository (Git or Fossil)
186: - `agent-workspace/` - Working directory where agent makes edits (plain files, not a repository)
187: 
188: **Note:** The `agent-workspace/` was previously called `checkout/` but was renamed to clarify its purpose as a working directory rather than a repository checkout.
189: 
190: ## Commit and Push Flow
191: 
192: When you click "Commit" in a session, the system performs a 4-step commit flow:
193: 
194: 1. **Sync** (`fossil up`) - Synchronizes the agent-workspace with the latest changes from repo.fossil
195: 2. **Copy** (clean slate) - Copies all files from agent-workspace to upstream/ directory, removing old files
196: 3. **Commit** - Commits changes in the upstream/ directory with message "Mimo commit at <timestamp>"
197: 4. **Push** - Pushes the commit to the remote repository
198: 
199: The commit flow preserves VCS metadata (`.git/` or `.fossil`) during the copy operation.
200: 
201: ### Breaking Changes
202: 
203: **Old sessions need recreation**: Sessions created before the agent-workspace rename (v1.x) stored `checkoutPath` in session.yaml. These sessions will need to be recreated to work with the new commit flow.
204: 
205: ## Development
206: 
207: ```bash
208: # Run tests
209: bun test
210: 
211: # Run with hot reload
212: bun run dev
213: 
214: # Build for production
215: bun run build
216: ```
217: 
218: ## License
219: 
220: MIT License - see LICENSE file for details.
221: 
222: ## Contributing
223: 
224: Contributions are welcome! Please read CONTRIBUTING.md for guidelines.

(End of file - total 224 lines)
</content>
````

<content>1: import { watch, existsSync, mkdirSync } from "fs";
2: import { join } from "path";
3: import { spawn } from "child_process";
4: import { SessionInfo, FileChange, ModelState, ModeState } from "./types";
5: 
6: export interface SessionCallbacks {
7:   onFileChange: (sessionId: string, changes: FileChange[]) => void;
8:   onSessionError: (sessionId: string, error: string) => void;
9: }
10: 
11: export class SessionManager {
12:   private sessions: Map<string, SessionInfo> = new Map();
13:   private pendingChanges: Map<string, FileChange[]> = new Map();
14:   private changeTimeouts: Map<string, NodeJS.Timeout> = new Map();
15:   private callbacks: SessionCallbacks;
16:   private workDir: string;
17: 
18:   constructor(workDir: string, callbacks: SessionCallbacks) {
19:     this.workDir = workDir;
20:     this.callbacks = callbacks;
21:   }
22: 
23:   getSession(sessionId: string): SessionInfo | undefined {
24:     return this.sessions.get(sessionId);
25:   }
26: 
27:   getAllSessions(): SessionInfo[] {
28:     return Array.from(this.sessions.values());
29:   }
30: 
31:   async createSession(
32:     sessionId: string,
33:     fossilUrl: string,
34:     fossilUser?: string,
35:     fossilPassword?: string
36:   ): Promise<SessionInfo> {
37:     const checkoutPath = join(this.workDir, sessionId);
38: 
39:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Creating session ${sessionId}`);
40:     console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Fossil URL: ${fossilUrl}`);
41:     console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Checkout: ${checkoutPath}`);
42: 
43:     // Clone/checkout logic handled by platform via fossil server
44:     // Just ensure the checkout directory exists
45:     if (!existsSync(checkoutPath)) {
46:       mkdirSync(checkoutPath, { recursive: true });
47:     }
48: 
49:     const sessionInfo: SessionInfo = {
50:       sessionId,
51:       checkoutPath,
52:       fossilUrl,
53:       fossilUser,
54:       fossilPassword,
55:       acpProcess: null,
56:       fileWatcher: null,
57:     };
58: 
59:     this.sessions.set(sessionId, sessionInfo);
60: 
61:     // Start file watcher
62:     this.startFileWatcher(sessionId, checkoutPath);
63: 
64:     return sessionInfo;
65:   }
66: 
67:   setSessionAcpProcess(sessionId: string, process: any): void {
68:     const session = this.sessions.get(sessionId);
69:     if (session) {
70:       session.acpProcess = process;
71:     }
72:   }
73: 
74:   setSessionState(
75:     sessionId: string,
76:     modelState?: ModelState,
77:     modeState?: ModeState
78:   ): void {
79:     const session = this.sessions.get(sessionId);
80:     if (session) {
81:       session.modelState = modelState;
82:       session.modeState = modeState;
83:     }
84:   }
85: 
86:   private startFileWatcher(sessionId: string, checkoutPath: string): void {
87:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Starting file watcher for session ${sessionId}`);
88: 
89:     const watcher = watch(
90:       checkoutPath,
91:       { recursive: true },
92:       (eventType: string, filename: string | null) => {
93:         if (!filename) return;
94: 
95:         // Skip hidden files and common ignore patterns
96:         if (
97:           filename.startsWith(".") ||
98:           filename.includes("/.") ||
99:           filename.includes("node_modules") ||
100:           filename.includes("__pycache__") ||
101:           filename.endsWith(".tmp") ||
102:           filename.endsWith("~")
103:         ) {
104:           return;
105:         }
106: 
107:         const change: FileChange = {
108:           path: filename,
109:           isNew: eventType === "rename",
110:           deleted: false,
111:         };
112: 
113:         const changes = this.pendingChanges.get(sessionId) || [];
114:         changes.push(change);
115:         this.pendingChanges.set(sessionId, changes);
116: 
117:         const existingTimeout = this.changeTimeouts.get(sessionId);
118:         if (existingTimeout) {
119:           clearTimeout(existingTimeout);
120:         }
121: 
122:         const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
123:           this.flushPendingChanges(sessionId);
124:         }, 500);
125:         this.changeTimeouts.set(sessionId, timeout);
126:       }
127:     );
128: 
129:     const session = this.sessions.get(sessionId);
130:     if (session) {
131:       session.fileWatcher = watcher;
132:     }
133:   }
134: 
135:   private flushPendingChanges(sessionId: string): void {
136:     const changes = this.pendingChanges.get(sessionId);
137:     if (!changes || changes.length === 0) return;
138: 
139:     this.pendingChanges.set(sessionId, []);
140:     this.changeTimeouts.delete(sessionId);
141: 
142:     // Deduplicate changes
143:     const uniqueChanges = new Map<string, FileChange>();
144:     for (const change of changes) {
145:       uniqueChanges.set(change.path, change);
146:     }
147: 
148:     this.callbacks.onFileChange(
149:       sessionId,
150:       Array.from(uniqueChanges.values())
151:     );
152:   }
153: 
154:   terminateSession(sessionId: string): void {
155:     const session = this.sessions.get(sessionId);
156:     if (!session) return;
157: 
158:     if (session.acpProcess) {
159:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Killing ACP process for ${sessionId}`);
160:       session.acpProcess.kill("SIGTERM");
161:     }
162: 
163:     if (session.fileWatcher) {
164:       session.fileWatcher.close();
165:     }
166: 
167:     // Clear any pending changes
168:     const timeout = this.changeTimeouts.get(sessionId);
169:     if (timeout) {
170:       clearTimeout(timeout);
171:       this.changeTimeouts.delete(sessionId);
172:     }
173:     this.pendingChanges.delete(sessionId);
174: 
175:     this.sessions.delete(sessionId);
176:   }
177: 
178:   terminateAll(): void {
179:     for (const sessionId of this.sessions.keys()) {
180:       this.terminateSession(sessionId);
181:     }
182:   }
183: }

(End of file - total 183 lines)

<content>1: import * as acp from "@agentclientprotocol/sdk";
2: import { IAcpProvider, NewSessionResponse } from "./types";
3: import { ModelState, ModeState } from "../types";
4: 
5: export interface AcpClientCallbacks {
6:   onThoughtStart: (sessionId: string) => void;
7:   onThoughtChunk: (sessionId: string, content: string) => void;
8:   onThoughtEnd: (sessionId: string) => void;
9:   onMessageChunk: (sessionId: string, content: string) => void;
10:   onUsageUpdate: (sessionId: string, usage: any) => void;
11:   onGenericUpdate: (sessionId: string, content: string) => void;
12: }
13: 
14: export interface AcpClientSession {
15:   sessionId: string;
16:   acpSessionId: string;
17:   connection: acp.ClientSideConnection;
18:   modelState?: ModelState;
19:   modeState?: ModeState;
20:   currentThoughtBuffer?: string;
21: }
22: 
23: export class AcpClient {
24:   private provider: IAcpProvider;
25:   private sessionId: string;
26:   private callbacks: AcpClientCallbacks;
27:   private session: AcpClientSession | null = null;
28: 
29:   constructor(
30:     provider: IAcpProvider,
31:     sessionId: string,
32:     callbacks: AcpClientCallbacks
33:   ) {
34:     this.provider = provider;
35:     this.sessionId = sessionId;
36:     this.callbacks = callbacks;
37:   }
38: 
39:   get acpSessionId(): string | undefined {
40:     return this.session?.acpSessionId;
41:   }
42: 
43:   get modelState(): ModelState | undefined {
44:     return this.session?.modelState;
45:   }
46: 
47:   get modeState(): ModeState | undefined {
48:     return this.session?.modeState;
49:   }
50: 
51:   async initialize(
52:     cwd: string,
53:     input: WritableStream<Uint8Array>,
54:     output: ReadableStream<Uint8Array>
55:   ): Promise<NewSessionResponse> {
56:     const stream = acp.ndJsonStream(input, output);
57: 
58:     // Create client with update handlers
59:     const client: acp.Client = {
60:       requestPermission: async () => ({
61:         outcome: { outcome: "approved", options: ["allow"] },
62:       }),
63:       sessionUpdate: async (params) => {
64:         this.handleSessionUpdate(params.update as any);
65:       },
66:     };
67: 
68:     const connection = new acp.ClientSideConnection(() => client, stream);
69: 
70:     // Initialize connection
71:     const initResponse = await connection.initialize({
72:       protocolVersion: acp.PROTOCOL_VERSION,
73:       clientInfo: { name: "mimo-agent", version: "0.1.0" },
74:     });
75: 
76:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] ACP initialized: ${initResponse.protocolVersion}`);
77: 
78:     // Create session
79:     const sessionResponse = await connection.newSession({
80:       cwd,
81:       mcpServers: [],
82:     });
83: 
84:     // Extract state using provider
85:     const state = this.provider.extractState(
86:       sessionResponse as NewSessionResponse
87:     );
88: 
89:     // Store session info
90:     this.session = {
91:       sessionId: this.sessionId,
92:       acpSessionId: sessionResponse.sessionId,
93:       connection,
94:       modelState: state.modelState,
95:       modeState: state.modeState,
96:     };
97: 
98:     return sessionResponse as NewSessionResponse;
99:   }
100: 
101:   private handleSessionUpdate(update: any): void {
102:     const updateType = update?.sessionUpdate;
103: 
104:     if (!this.session) return;
105: 
106:     const mappedType = this.provider.mapUpdateType(updateType);
107: 
108:     // Skip updates we don't care about
109:     if (mappedType === null) return;
110: 
111:     switch (mappedType) {
112:       case "thought_chunk":
113:         // Send thought start on first chunk
114:         if (!this.session.currentThoughtBuffer) {
115:           this.session.currentThoughtBuffer = "";
116:           this.callbacks.onThoughtStart(this.sessionId);
117:         }
118:         this.session.currentThoughtBuffer += update.content?.text || "";
119:         this.callbacks.onThoughtChunk(
120:           this.sessionId,
121:           update.content?.text || ""
122:         );
123:         break;
124: 
125:       case "message_chunk":
126:         // End thought buffering if active
127:         if (this.session.currentThoughtBuffer) {
128:           this.callbacks.onThoughtEnd(this.sessionId);
129:           this.session.currentThoughtBuffer = "";
130:         }
131:         this.callbacks.onMessageChunk(
132:           this.sessionId,
133:           update.content?.text || ""
134:         );
135:         break;
136: 
137:       case "usage_update":
138:         this.callbacks.onUsageUpdate(this.sessionId, {
139:           cost: update.cost || {},
140:           size: update.size,
141:           used: update.used,
142:         });
143:         break;
144: 
145:       default:
146:         this.callbacks.onGenericUpdate(this.sessionId, updateType || "update");
147:     }
148:   }
149: 
150:   async prompt(content: string): Promise<acp.PromptResponse> {
151:     if (!this.session) {
152:       throw new Error("Session not initialized");
153:     }
154: 
155:     return this.session.connection.prompt({
156:       sessionId: this.session.acpSessionId,
157:       prompt: [{ type: "text", text: content }],
158:     });
159:   }
160: 
161:   async setModel(modelId: string): Promise<void> {
162:     if (!this.session) {
163:       throw new Error("Session not initialized");
164:     }
165: 
166:     if (!this.session.modelState) {
167:       throw new Error("Model state not available");
168:     }
169: 
170:     await this.provider.setModel(
171:       this.session.connection,
172:       this.session.acpSessionId,
173:       modelId,
174:       this.session.modelState.optionId
175:     );
176: 
177:     // Update local state
178:     this.session.modelState.currentModelId = modelId;
179:   }
180: 
181:   async setMode(modeId: string): Promise<void> {
182:     if (!this.session) {
183:       throw new Error("Session not initialized");
184:     }
185: 
186:     if (!this.session.modeState) {
187:       throw new Error("Mode state not available");
188:     }
189: 
190:     await this.provider.setMode(
191:       this.session.connection,
192:       this.session.acpSessionId,
193:       modeId,
194:       this.session.modeState.optionId
195:     );
196: 
197:     // Update local state
198:     this.session.modeState.currentModeId = modeId;
199:   }
200: }

47:   private getSessionPath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
48:     return join(getPaths().projects, projectId, "sessions", sessionId);
49:   }
50: 
51:   private getSessionFilePath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
52:     return join(this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId), "session.yaml");
53:   }
54: 
55:   private getUpstreamPath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
56:     return join(this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId), "upstream");
57:   }
58: 
59:   private getAgentWorkspacePath(projectId: string, sessionId: string): string {
60:     return join(this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId), "agent-workspace");
61:   }
62: 
63:   private generateId(): string {
64:     return crypto.randomUUID();
65:   }
66: 
67:   async create(input: CreateSessionInput): Promise<Session> {
68:     const id = this.generateId();
69:     const sessionPath = this.getSessionPath(input.projectId, id);
70:     const upstreamPath = this.getUpstreamPath(input.projectId, id);
71:     const agentWorkspacePath = this.getAgentWorkspacePath(input.projectId, id);
72: 
73:     // Create session directory
74:     if (!existsSync(sessionPath)) {
75:       mkdirSync(sessionPath, { recursive: true });
76:     }
77: 
78:     // Create upstream directory
79:     if (!existsSync(upstreamPath)) {
80:       mkdirSync(upstreamPath, { recursive: true });
81:     }
82: 
83:     // Create agent-workspace directory
84:     if (!existsSync(agentWorkspacePath)) {
85:       mkdirSync(agentWorkspacePath, { recursive: true });
86:     }
87: 
88:     const now = new Date().toISOString();
89:     const sessionData: SessionData = {
90:       id,
91:       name: input.name,
92:       projectId: input.projectId,
93:       owner: input.owner,
94:       upstreamPath,
95:       agentWorkspacePath,
96:       assignedAgentId: input.assignedAgentId,
97:       status: "active",
98:       port: null,
99:       createdAt: now,
100:       updatedAt: now,
101:     };
102: 
103:     writeFileSync(
104:       this.getSessionFilePath(input.projectId, id),
105:       dump(sessionData),
106:       "utf-8"
107:     );
108: 
109:     return {
110:       ...sessionData,
111:       createdAt: new Date(sessionData.createdAt),
112:       updatedAt: new Date(sessionData.updatedAt),
113:     };
114:   }

116:   async findById(sessionId: string): Promise<Session | null> {
117:     // Search across all projects for the session
118:     const Paths = getPaths();
119:     if (!existsSync(Paths.projects)) {
120:       return null;
121:     }
122: 
123:     const projectEntries = readdirSync(Paths.projects, { withFileTypes: true });
124:     
125:     for (const projectEntry of projectEntries) {
126:       if (projectEntry.isDirectory()) {
127:         const sessionsDir = join(Paths.projects, projectEntry.name, "sessions");
128:         if (existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
129:           const sessionFile = join(sessionsDir, sessionId, "session.yaml");
130:           if (existsSync(sessionFile)) {
131:             const content = readFileSync(sessionFile, "utf-8");
132:             const data = load(content) as SessionData;
133:             // Handle migration from checkoutPath to agentWorkspacePath
134:             const sessionData = {
135:               ...data,
136:               agentWorkspacePath: data.agentWorkspacePath || (data as any).checkoutPath,
137:             };
138:             return {
139:               ...sessionData,
140:               createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
141:               updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
142:             };
143:           }
144:         }
145:       }
146:     }
147: 
148:     return null;
149:   }

172:   async listByProject(projectId: string): Promise<Session[]> {
173:     const sessionsDir = join(getPaths().projects, projectId, "sessions");
174:     if (!existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
175:       return [];
176:     }
177: 
178:     const entries = readdirSync(sessionsDir, { withFileTypes: true });
179:     const sessions: Session[] = [];
180: 
181:     for (const entry of entries) {
182:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
183:         const sessionFile = join(sessionsDir, entry.name, "session.yaml");
184:         if (existsSync(sessionFile)) {
185:           const content = readFileSync(sessionFile, "utf-8");
186:           const data = load(content) as SessionData;
187:           // Handle migration from checkoutPath to agentWorkspacePath
188:           const sessionData = {
189:             ...data,
190:             agentWorkspacePath: data.agentWorkspacePath || (data as any).checkoutPath,
191:           };
192:           sessions.push({
193:             ...sessionData,
194:             createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
195:             updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
196:           });
197:         }
198:       }
199:     }
200: 
201:     return sessions.sort((a, b) => b.createdAt.getTime() - a.createdAt.getTime());
202:   }
203: 
204:   async findByAssignedAgentId(agentId: string): Promise<Session[]> {
205:     const Paths = getPaths();

207:       return [];
208:     }
209: 
210:     const projectEntries = readdirSync(Paths.projects, { withFileTypes: true });

228:                 };

230:                   sessions.push({
231:                     ...sessionData,
232:                     createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
233:                     updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
234:                   });
235:                 }
236:               }
237:             }
238:           }
239:         }
240:       }
241:     }
242: 
243:     return sessions.sort((a, b) => b.createdAt.getTime() - a.createdAt.getTime());
244:   }
245: 
246:   async update(sessionId: string, updates: Partial<Omit<SessionData, "id" | "createdAt">>): Promise<Session | null> {
247:     const session = await this.findById(sessionId);
248:     if (!session) return null;
249: 
250:     const updatedData: SessionData = {
251:       ...session,
252:       ...updates,
253:       updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),

261:       createdAt: new Date(updatedData.createdAt),
262:       updatedAt: new Date(updatedData.updatedAt),
263:     };
264:   }
265: 
266:   async delete(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
267:     const sessionPath = this.getSessionPath(projectId, sessionId);
268:     
269:     // Delete entire session directory (includes upstream/, agent-workspace/, repo.fossil, session.yaml)
270:     if (existsSync(sessionPath)) {
271:       this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(sessionPath);
272:     }
273:   }
274: 
275:   private deleteDirectoryRecursive(dirPath: string): void {
276:     if (!existsSync(dirPath)) return;
277: 
278:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
279:     
280:     for (const entry of entries) {
281:       const entryPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
282:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
283:         this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(entryPath);
284:       } else {
285:         unlinkSync(entryPath);
286:       }
287:     }
288: 
289:     rmdirSync(dirPath);
290:   }
291: 
292:   async exists(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<boolean> {
293:     return existsSync(this.getSessionFilePath(projectId, sessionId));
294:   }
295: }
296: 
297: export const sessionRepository = new SessionRepository();

(End of file - total 297 lines)

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 00:48:44)

Excellent! Now I'm getting a clearer picture. Let me understand the session management:

1. **mimo-platform sessions** - Stored in session.yaml files, persisted to disk. Each session has a `sessionId` (UUID generated)
2. **mimo-agent sessions** - Managed in-memory by SessionManager, keyed by sessionId
3. **ACP sessions** - Created by AcpClient, has its own `acpSessionId` which is different

The problem is:
- When mimo-agent restarts, its in-memory session data is lost
- Even though chat.jsonl persists the messages, the ACP session ID is lost
- When the agent reconnects, it creates a NEW ACP session, breaking continuity

Let me look at how the chat and WebSocket work, and how the agent starts up.

<content>1: import { join } from "path";
2: import { existsSync, mkdirSync, appendFileSync, readFileSync } from "fs";

4: 
5: export interface ChatMessage {
6:   role: "user" | "assistant" | "system";
7:   content: string;
8:   timestamp: string;
9:   metadata?: Record<string, unknown>;
10: }
11: 
12: export class ChatService {
13:   private getChatPath(sessionId: string): string {
14:     // Store chat in the session directory
15:     const Paths = getPaths();
16:     const sessionDir = this.findSessionDir(sessionId);
17:     if (!sessionDir) {
18:       throw new Error(`Session ${sessionId} not found`);
19:     }
20:     return join(sessionDir, "chat.jsonl");
21:   }
22: 
23:   private findSessionDir(sessionId: string): string | null {
24:     const Paths = getPaths();
25:     if (!existsSync(Paths.projects)) {
26:       return null;
27:     }
28: 
29:     const { readdirSync } = require("fs");
30:     const projectEntries = readdirSync(Paths.projects, { withFileTypes: true });
31:     
32:     for (const projectEntry of projectEntries) {
33:       if (projectEntry.isDirectory()) {
34:         const sessionsDir = join(Paths.projects, projectEntry.name, "sessions");
35:         if (existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
36:           const sessionDir = join(sessionsDir, sessionId);
37:           if (existsSync(sessionDir)) {
38:             return sessionDir;
39:           }
40:         }
41:       }
42:     }
43: 
44:     return null;
45:   }
46: 
47:   async saveMessage(sessionId: string, message: ChatMessage): Promise<void> {
48:     const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
49:     const line = JSON.stringify(message) + "\n";
50:     appendFileSync(chatPath, line, "utf-8");
51:   }
52: 
53:   async loadHistory(sessionId: string): Promise<ChatMessage[]> {
54:     try {
55:       const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
56:       if (!existsSync(chatPath)) {
57:         return [];
58:       }
59: 
60:       const content = readFileSync(chatPath, "utf-8");
61:       const lines = content.trim().split("\n").filter(line => line);
62:       
63:       return lines.map((line) => JSON.parse(line) as ChatMessage);
64:     } catch {
65:       return [];
66:     }
67:   }
68: 
69:   async appendToHistory(sessionId: string, messages: ChatMessage[]): Promise<void> {
70:     const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
71:     const lines = messages.map((msg) => JSON.stringify(msg)).join("\n") + "\n";
72:     appendFileSync(chatPath, lines, "utf-8");
73:   }
74: 
75:   async clearHistory(sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
76:     const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
77:     if (existsSync(chatPath)) {
78:       const { unlinkSync } = require("fs");
79:       unlinkSync(chatPath);
80:     }
81:   }
82: }
83:

28: 
29:   constructor() {
30:     this.config = this.parseArgs();
31:     this.sessionManager = new SessionManager(this.config.workDir, {
32:       onFileChange: (sessionId, changes) => {
33:         this.send({
34:           type: "file_changed",
35:           sessionId,
36:           files: changes,
37:           timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
38:         });
39:       },
40:       onSessionError: (sessionId, error) => {
41:         this.send({
42:           type: "session_error",
43:           sessionId,
44:           error,

46:         });
47:       },

52:   private parseArgs(): AgentConfig {
53:     const args = process.argv.slice(2);
54:     const config: Partial<AgentConfig> = {};
55: 
56:     for (let i = 0; i < args.length; i++) {
57:       const arg = args[i];
58:       if (arg === "--token" && i + 1 < args.length) {
59:         config.token = args[++i];
60:       } else if (arg === "--platform" && i + 1 < args.length) {
61:         config.platform = args[++i];
62:       } else if (arg === "--workdir" && i + 1 < args.length) {
63:         config.workDir = args[++i];
64:       }
65:     }
66: 
67:     if (!config.token) {
68:       throw new Error("Missing required argument: --token");
69:     }
70:     if (!config.platform) {
71:       throw new Error("Missing required argument: --platform");
72:     }
73: 
74:     if (!config.workDir) {
75:       config.workDir = process.cwd();
76:     }
77: 
78:     return config as AgentConfig;
79:   }
80: 
81:   async start(): Promise<void> {
82:     console.log("[mimo-agent] Starting...");
83:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Platform: ${this.config.platform}`);
84:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] WorkDir: ${this.config.workDir}`);
85: 
86:     await this.connect();
87:     this.setupShutdownHandlers();
88:   }
89: 
90:   private async connect(): Promise<void> {
91:     const wsUrl = `${this.config.platform}?token=${this.config.token}`;
92: 
93:     return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
94:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Connecting to ${this.config.platform}...`);
95: 
96:       this.ws = new WebSocket(wsUrl);
97: 
98:       this.ws.on("open", () => {
99:         console.log("[mimo-agent] Connected to platform");
100:         this.reconnectAttempts = 0;
101: 
102:         this.send({
103:           type: "agent_ready",
104:           workdir: this.config.workDir,
105:           timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
106:         });
107: 
108:         resolve();
109:       });
110: 
111:       this.ws.on("message", (data: Buffer) => {
112:         try {
113:           const message = JSON.parse(data.toString());
114:           this.handleMessage(message);
115:         } catch (error) {
116:           console.error("[mimo-agent] Failed to parse message:", error);
117:         }
118:       });
119: 
120:       this.ws.on("close", () => {
121:         console.log("[mimo-agent] Disconnected");
122:         this.handleDisconnect();
123:       });
124: 
125:       this.ws.on("error", (error: Error) => {
126:         console.error("[mimo-agent] WebSocket error:", error.message);
127:         reject(error);
128:       });
129: 
130:       setTimeout(() => {
131:         if (this.ws?.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN) {
132:           reject(new Error("Connection timeout"));
133:         }
134:       }, 10000);
135:     });
136:   }
137: 
138:   private handleMessage(message: any): void {
139:     switch (message.type) {
140:       case "ping":
141:         this.send({ type: "pong" });
142:         break;
143: 
144:       case "session_ready":
145:         this.handleSessionReady(message);
146:         break;
147: 
148:       case "acp_request":
149:         this.handleAcpRequest(message);
150:         break;
151: 
152:       case "cancel_request":
153:         this.handleCancelRequest(message);
154:         break;
155: 
156:       case "file_sync_request":
157:         this.handleFileSyncRequest(message);
158:         break;
159: 
160:       case "user_message":
161:         this.handleUserMessage(message);
162:         break;
163: 
164:       case "set_model":
165:         this.handleSetModel(message);
166:         break;
167: 
168:       case "set_mode":
169:         this.handleSetMode(message);
170:         break;
171: 
172:       case "request_state":
173:         this.handleRequestState(message);
174:         break;
175: 
176:       default:
177:         console.log("[mimo-agent] Unknown message type:", message.type);
178:     }
179:   }
180: 
181:   private async handleSessionReady(message: any): Promise<void> {
182:     const { platformUrl, sessions } = message;
183: 
184:     if (!sessions || sessions.length === 0) {
185:       console.log("[mimo-agent] No sessions assigned");
186:       return;
187:     }
188: 
189:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Received ${sessions.length} session(s)`);
190:     const sessionIds: string[] = [];
191: 
192:     for (const session of sessions) {
193:       const { sessionId, port, agentWorkspaceUser, agentWorkspacePassword } = session;
194: 
195:       try {
196:         const checkoutPath = join(this.config.workDir, sessionId);
197:         const platformHost = platformUrl
198:           .replace(/^https?:\/\//, "")
199:           .replace(/\/+$/, "");
200:         const fossilUrl = `http://${platformHost.split(":")[0]}:${port}/`;
201: 
202:         // Setup checkout directory with credentials
203:         await this.setupCheckout(sessionId, checkoutPath, fossilUrl, agentWorkspaceUser, agentWorkspacePassword);
204: 
205:         // Create session with credentials
206:         const sessionInfo = await this.sessionManager.createSession(
207:           sessionId,
208:           fossilUrl,
209:           agentWorkspaceUser,
210:           agentWorkspacePassword
211:         );
212: 
213:         // Spawn ACP process
214:         this.spawnAcpProcess(sessionInfo);
215: 
216:         sessionIds.push(sessionId);
217:         console.log(`[mimo-agent] Session ${sessionId} ready`);
218:       } catch (error) {
219:         console.error(
220:           `[mimo-agent] Failed to setup session ${sessionId}:`,
221:           error
222:         );
223:         this.send({
224:           type: "session_error",
225:           sessionId,
226:           error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
227:           timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
228:         });
229:       }
230:     }
231: 
232:     this.send({
233:       type: "agent_sessions_ready",
234:       sessionIds,
235:       timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
236:     });
237:   }
238: 
239:   private async setupCheckout(
240:     sessionId: string,
241:     checkoutPath: string,
242:     fossilUrl: string,
243:     agentWorkspaceUser?: string,
244:     agentWorkspacePassword?: string
245:   ): Promise<void> {
246:     const repoPath = join(checkoutPath, "..", `${sessionId}.fossil`);
247: 
248:     if (existsSync(repoPath)) {
249:       console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Fossil repo exists, opening`);
250:       if (!existsSync(checkoutPath)) {
251:         mkdirSync(checkoutPath, { recursive: true });
252:       }
253:       try {
254:         execSync(`fossil open ${repoPath}`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
255:       } catch {
256:         // Already open or error, continue
257:       }
258:       // Update remote URL to new port/credentials
259:       if (agentWorkspaceUser && agentWorkspacePassword) {
260:         const url = new URL(fossilUrl);
261:         url.username = agentWorkspaceUser;
262:         url.password = agentWorkspacePassword;
263:         const remoteUrl = url.toString();
264:         console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Updating remote URL to: ${url.protocol}//${url.username}:****@${url.host}/`);
265:         try {
266:           execSync(`fossil remote-url ${remoteUrl}`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
267:         } catch {
268:           // Ignore error, may already be correct
269:         }
270:         // Ensure local password matches server password
271:         try {
272:           execSync(
273:             `fossil user password ${agentWorkspaceUser} ${agentWorkspacePassword}`,
274:             { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
275:           );
276:           console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Updated local user password`);
277:         } catch {
278:           // Ignore error
279:         }
280:         // Update/add named remote "server" with credentials
281:         try {
282:           // Remove existing remote if exists, then add new one
283:           try {
284:             execSync(`fossil remote rm server`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
285:           } catch {
286:             // Remote may not exist, ignore
287:           }
288:           execSync(
289:             `fossil remote add server ${remoteUrl}`,
290:             { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
291:           );
292:           console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Updated remote 'server'`);
293:           // Do a sync using the named remote to verify credentials work
294:           execSync(
295:             `fossil sync server`,
296:             { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
297:           );
298:           console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Verified sync with remote 'server'`);
299:         } catch {
300:           // Ignore error
301:         }
302:       }
303:     } else if (existsSync(join(checkoutPath, ".fossil"))) {
304:       console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Checkout exists, ensuring open`);
305:       try {
306:         execSync(`fossil open`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
307:       } catch {
308:         // Already open or error, continue
309:       }
310:       // Update remote URL to new port/credentials
311:       if (agentWorkspaceUser && agentWorkspacePassword) {
312:         const url = new URL(fossilUrl);
313:         url.username = agentWorkspaceUser;
314:         url.password = agentWorkspacePassword;
315:         const remoteUrl = url.toString();
316:         console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Updating remote URL to: ${url.protocol}//${url.username}:****@${url.host}/`);
317:         try {
318:           execSync(`fossil remote-url ${remoteUrl}`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
319:         } catch {
320:           // Ignore error, may already be correct
321:         }
322:         // Ensure local password matches server password
323:         try {
324:           execSync(
325:             `fossil user password ${agentWorkspaceUser} ${agentWorkspacePassword}`,
326:             { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
327:           );
328:           console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Updated local user password`);
329:         } catch {
330:           // Ignore error
331:         }
332:         // Update/add named remote "server" with credentials
333:         try {
334:           // Remove existing remote if exists, then add new one
335:           try {
336:             execSync(`fossil remote rm server`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
337:           } catch {
338:             // Remote may not exist, ignore
339:           }
340:           execSync(
341:             `fossil remote add server ${remoteUrl}`,
342:             { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
343:           );
344:           console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Updated remote 'server'`);
345:           // Do a sync using the named remote to verify credentials work
346:           execSync(
347:             `fossil sync server`,
348:             { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
349:           );
350:           console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Verified sync with remote 'server'`);
351:         } catch {
352:           // Ignore error
353:         }
354:       }
355:     } else {
356:       console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Cloning from fossil`);
357:       // Use credentials in URL if available
358:       let cloneUrl = fossilUrl;
359:       if (agentWorkspaceUser && agentWorkspacePassword) {
360:         const url = new URL(fossilUrl);
361:         url.username = agentWorkspaceUser;
362:         url.password = agentWorkspacePassword;
363:         cloneUrl = url.toString();
364:         console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Using authenticated URL: ${url.protocol}//${url.username}:****@${url.host}/`);
365:       }
366:       execSync(`fossil clone ${cloneUrl} ${repoPath}`, { stdio: "pipe" });
367:       if (!existsSync(checkoutPath)) {
368:         mkdirSync(checkoutPath, { recursive: true });
369:       }
370:       // Open without sync first, then set remote with credentials
371:       execSync(`fossil open --nosync ${repoPath}`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
372:       // Set remote URL with credentials for future syncs
373:       execSync(`fossil remote-url ${cloneUrl}`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
374:       // Set local password to match server password (fossil creates local admin with random password)
375:       if (agentWorkspaceUser && agentWorkspacePassword) {
376:         execSync(
377:           `fossil user password ${agentWorkspaceUser} ${agentWorkspacePassword}`,
378:           { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
379:         );
380:         // Add a named remote "server" with credentials embedded
381:         execSync(
382:           `fossil remote add server ${cloneUrl}`,
383:           { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
384:         );
385:         // Do an initial sync using the named remote with credentials
386:         execSync(
387:           `fossil sync server`,
388:           { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
389:         );
390:       }
391:     }
392:   }
393: 
394:   private spawnAcpProcess(session: any): void {
395:     const sessionInfo = this.sessionManager.getSession(session.sessionId);
396:     if (!sessionInfo) return;
397: 
398:     // Terminate existing
399:     if (sessionInfo.acpProcess) {
400:       console.log(
401:         `[mimo-agent] Terminating existing ACP for ${session.sessionId}`
402:       );
403:       sessionInfo.acpProcess.kill();
404:     }
405: 
406:     const spawnResult = this.provider.spawn(sessionInfo.checkoutPath);
407:     const process = spawnResult.process;
408:     this.sessionManager.setSessionAcpProcess(session.sessionId, process);
409: 
410:     // Create ACP client
411:     const acpClient = new AcpClient(
412:       this.provider,
413:       session.sessionId,
414:       {
415:         onThoughtStart: (sessionId) => {
416:           this.send({
417:             type: "thought_start",
418:             sessionId,
419:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
420:           });
421:         },
422:         onThoughtChunk: (sessionId, content) => {
423:           this.send({
424:             type: "thought_chunk",
425:             sessionId,
426:             content,
427:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
428:           });
429:         },
430:         onThoughtEnd: (sessionId) => {
431:           this.send({
432:             type: "thought_end",
433:             sessionId,
434:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
435:           });
436:         },
437:         onMessageChunk: (sessionId, content) => {
438:           this.send({
439:             type: "message_chunk",
440:             sessionId,
441:             content,
442:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
443:           });
444:         },
445:         onUsageUpdate: (sessionId, usage) => {
446:           this.send({
447:             type: "usage_update",
448:             sessionId,
449:             usage,
450:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
451:           });
452:         },
453:         onGenericUpdate: (sessionId, content) => {
454:           this.send({
455:             type: "acp_response",
456:             sessionId,
457:             content,
458:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
459:           });
460:         },
461:       }
462:     );
463: 
464:     // Initialize ACP client
465:     acpClient
466:       .initialize(
467:         sessionInfo.checkoutPath,
468:         toWebWritable(spawnResult.stdin),
469:         toWebReadable(spawnResult.stdout)
470:       )
471:       .then(() => {
472:         console.log(`[mimo-agent] ACP client ready for ${session.sessionId}`);
473:         this.acpClients.set(session.sessionId, acpClient);
474: 
475:         // Update session state
476:         this.sessionManager.setSessionState(
477:           session.sessionId,
478:           acpClient.modelState,
479:           acpClient.modeState
480:         );
481: 
482:         // Send session initialized
483:         this.send({
484:           type: "session_initialized",
485:           sessionId: session.sessionId,
486:           modelState: acpClient.modelState,
487:           modeState: acpClient.modeState,
488:           timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
489:         });
490:       })
491:       .catch((err) => {
492:         console.error(
493:           `[mimo-agent] ACP init error for ${session.sessionId}:`,
494:           err
495:         );
496:       });
497: 
498:     // Handle process events
499:     process.stderr?.on("data", (data: Buffer) => {
500:       console.error(
501:         `[mimo-agent] ACP stderr (${session.sessionId}):`,
502:         data.toString()
503:       );
504:     });
505: 
506:     process.on("close", (code: number | null) => {
507:       console.log(
508:         `[mimo-agent] ACP exited for ${session.sessionId} with code ${code}`
509:       );
510:       this.acpClients.delete(session.sessionId);
511:       this.sessionManager.setSessionAcpProcess(session.sessionId, null);
512:     });
513: 
514:     process.on("error", (err: Error) => {
515:       console.error(
516:         `[mimo-agent] ACP process error for ${session.sessionId}:`,
517:         err.message
518:       );
519:       this.send({
520:         type: "session_error",
521:         sessionId: session.sessionId,
522:         error: `ACP process error: ${err.message}`,
523:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
524:       });
525:     });
526:   }
527: 
528:   private handleAcpRequest(message: any): void {
529:     const sessionId = message.sessionId;
530:     if (!sessionId) {
531:       console.log("[mimo-agent] No sessionId in acp_request");
532:       return;
533:     }
534: 
535:     const session = this.sessionManager.getSession(sessionId);
536:     if (!session) {
537:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Unknown session ${sessionId}`);
538:       return;
539:     }
540: 
541:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Restarting ACP for session ${sessionId}`);
542:     this.spawnAcpProcess(session);
543:   }
544: 
545:   private handleCancelRequest(message: any): void {
546:     const sessionId = message.sessionId;
547:     if (!sessionId) {
548:       console.log("[mimo-agent] No sessionId in cancel_request");
549:       return;
550:     }
551: 
552:     const session = this.sessionManager.getSession(sessionId);
553:     if (!session) {
554:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Unknown session ${sessionId}`);
555:       return;
556:     }
557: 
558:     if (session.acpProcess) {
559:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Cancelling ACP for ${sessionId}`);
560:       session.acpProcess.kill("SIGTERM");
561:       this.sessionManager.setSessionAcpProcess(sessionId, null);
562:       this.acpClients.delete(sessionId);
563: 
564:       this.send({
565:         type: "acp_cancelled",
566:         sessionId,
567:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
568:       });
569:     }
570:   }
571: 
572:   private handleFileSyncRequest(message: any): void {
573:     const sessionId = message.sessionId;
574:     console.log(
575:       `[mimo-agent] File sync for session ${sessionId || "unknown"}`
576:     );
577:   }
578: 
579:   private handleUserMessage(message: any): void {
580:     const sessionId = message.sessionId;
581:     const content = message.content;
582: 
583:     if (!sessionId) {
584:       console.log("[mimo-agent] No sessionId in user_message");
585:       return;
586:     }
587: 
588:     const acpClient = this.acpClients.get(sessionId);
589:     if (!acpClient) {
590:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] No ACP client for session ${sessionId}`);
591:       this.send({
592:         type: "error_response",
593:         sessionId,
594:         error: `No ACP connection for session: ${sessionId}`,
595:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
596:       });
597:       return;
598:     }
599: 
600:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Sending prompt for session ${sessionId}`);
601:     acpClient
602:       .prompt(content)
603:       .then(() => {
604:         console.log(`[mimo-agent] Prompt completed for ${sessionId}`);
605:       })
606:       .catch((err) => {
607:         console.error(`[mimo-agent] Prompt error:`, err);
608:         this.send({
609:           type: "error_response",
610:           sessionId,
611:           error: `ACP prompt error: ${err.message}`,
612:           timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
613:         });
614:       });
615:   }
616: 
617:   private async handleSetModel(message: any): Promise<void> {
618:     const { sessionId, modelId } = message;
619:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Set model for ${sessionId}: ${modelId}`);
620: 
621:     const acpClient = this.acpClients.get(sessionId);
622:     if (!acpClient) {
623:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] No ACP client for session ${sessionId}`);
624:       return;
625:     }
626: 
627:     try {
628:       await acpClient.setModel(modelId);
629: 
630:       this.send({
631:         type: "model_state",
632:         sessionId,
633:         modelState: acpClient.modelState,
634:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
635:       });
636: 
637:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Model changed to ${modelId}`);
638:     } catch (err: any) {
639:       console.error(`[mimo-agent] Failed to set model:`, err);
640:       this.send({
641:         type: "error_response",
642:         sessionId,
643:         error: `Failed to set model: ${err.message}`,
644:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
645:       });
646:     }
647:   }
648: 
649:   private async handleSetMode(message: any): Promise<void> {
650:     const { sessionId, modeId } = message;
651:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Set mode for ${sessionId}: ${modeId}`);
652: 
653:     const acpClient = this.acpClients.get(sessionId);
654:     if (!acpClient) {
655:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] No ACP client for session ${sessionId}`);
656:       return;
657:     }
658: 
659:     try {
660:       await acpClient.setMode(modeId);
661: 
662:       this.send({
663:         type: "mode_state",
664:         sessionId,
665:         modeState: acpClient.modeState,
666:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
667:       });
668: 
669:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Mode changed to ${modeId}`);
670:     } catch (err: any) {
671:       console.error(`[mimo-agent] Failed to set mode:`, err);
672:       this.send({
673:         type: "error_response",
674:         sessionId,
675:         error: `Failed to set mode: ${err.message}`,
676:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
677:       });
678:     }
679:   }
680: 
681:   private handleRequestState(message: any): void {
682:     const { sessionId } = message;
683:     const acpClient = this.acpClients.get(sessionId);
684: 
685:     if (!acpClient) {
686:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Unknown session ${sessionId} in request_state`);
687:       return;
688:     }
689: 
690:     this.send({
691:       type: "session_initialized",
692:       sessionId,
693:       modelState: acpClient.modelState,
694:       modeState: acpClient.modeState,
695:       timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
696:     });
697: 
698:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Sent state for session ${sessionId}`);
699:   }
700: 
701:   private handleDisconnect(): void {
702:     if (this.reconnectAttempts < this.maxReconnectAttempts) {
703:       this.reconnectAttempts++;
704:       const delay = this.reconnectDelay * Math.pow(2, this.reconnectAttempts - 1);
705:       console.log(
706:         `[mimo-agent] Reconnecting in ${delay}ms (attempt ${this.reconnectAttempts})...`
707:       );
708: 
709:       setTimeout(() => {
710:         this.connect().catch((error) => {
711:           console.error("[mimo-agent] Reconnect failed:", error.message);
712:         });
713:       }, delay);
714:     } else {
715:       console.error("[mimo-agent] Max reconnect attempts reached");
716:       process.exit(1);
717:     }
718:   }
719: 
720:   private send(message: any): void {
721:     if (this.ws?.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
722:       this.ws.send(JSON.stringify(message));
723:     } else {
724:       console.log("[mimo-agent] WebSocket not connected");
725:     }
726:   }
727: 
728:   private setupShutdownHandlers(): void {
729:     const shutdown = () => {
730:       console.log("[mimo-agent] Shutting down...");
731:       this.sessionManager.terminateAll();
732:       this.ws?.close();
733:       process.exit(0);
734:     };
735: 
736:     process.on("SIGTERM", shutdown);
737:     process.on("SIGINT", shutdown);
738:     process.on("SIGUSR2", shutdown);
739: 
740:     process.on("uncaughtException", (error) => {
741:       console.error("[mimo-agent] Uncaught exception:", error);
742:       shutdown();
743:     });
744:   }
745: }
746: 
747: const agent = new MimoAgent();
748: agent.start().catch((error) => {
749:   console.error("[mimo-agent] Failed to start:", error.message);
750:   process.exit(1);
751: });

<content>1: import { IAcpProvider, NewSessionResponse } from "../types";
2: import { ModelState, ModeState } from "../../types";
3: import { spawn, ChildProcess } from "child_process";
4: import { Readable, Writable } from "node:stream";
5: 
6: export class OpencodeProvider implements IAcpProvider {
7:   readonly name = "opencode";
8: 
9:   spawn(cwd: string): {
10:     process: ChildProcess;
11:     stdin: Writable;
12:     stdout: Readable;
13:     stderr?: Readable;
14:   } {
15:     const proc = spawn("opencode", ["acp"], {
16:       cwd,
17:       stdio: ["pipe", "pipe", "pipe"],
18:     });
19: 
20:     return {
21:       process: proc,
22:       stdin: proc.stdin!,
23:       stdout: proc.stdout!,
24:       stderr: proc.stderr!,
25:     };
26:   }
27: 
28:   extractState(
29:     response: NewSessionResponse
30:   ): {
31:     modelState?: ModelState;
32:     modeState?: ModeState;
33:   } {
34:     const result: { modelState?: ModelState; modeState?: ModeState } = {};
35: 
36:     // Try modern configOptions first
37:     if (response.configOptions) {
38:       const modelConfig = response.configOptions.find(
39:         (opt) => opt.category === "model" && opt.type === "select"
40:       );
41:       const modeConfig = response.configOptions.find(
42:         (opt) => opt.category === "mode" && opt.type === "select"
43:       );
44: 
45:       if (modelConfig && modelConfig.type === "select") {
46:         const availableOptions = Array.isArray(modelConfig.options)
47:           ? modelConfig.options.map((opt) => ({
48:               value: opt.value,
49:               name: opt.name,
50:               description: opt.description,
51:             }))
52:           : [];
53: 
54:         result.modelState = {
55:           currentModelId: modelConfig.currentValue || availableOptions[0]?.value || "",
56:           availableModels: availableOptions,
57:           optionId: modelConfig.id,
58:         };
59:       }
60: 
61:       if (modeConfig && modeConfig.type === "select") {
62:         const availableOptions = Array.isArray(modeConfig.options)
63:           ? modeConfig.options.map((opt) => ({
64:               value: opt.value,
65:               name: opt.name,
66:               description: opt.description,
67:             }))
68:           : [];
69: 
70:         result.modeState = {
71:           currentModeId: modeConfig.currentValue || availableOptions[0]?.value || "",
72:           availableModes: availableOptions,
73:           optionId: modeConfig.id,
74:         };
75:       }
76:     }
77:     // Fallback to legacy format (models/modes fields)
78:     else if (response.models) {
79:       // Extract model state from legacy 'models' field
80:       if (response.models) {
81:         const models = response.models;
82:         const availableOptions = Array.isArray(models.availableModels)
83:           ? models.availableModels.map((m) => ({
84:               value: m.modelId || m.id || "",
85:               name: m.name || m.modelId || m.id || "",
86:               description: m.description,
87:             }))
88:           : [];
89: 
90:         result.modelState = {
91:           currentModelId: models.currentModelId || availableOptions[0]?.value || "",
92:           availableModels: availableOptions,
93:           optionId: "model",
94:         };
95:       }
96: 
97:       // Extract mode state from legacy 'modes' field
98:       if (response.modes) {
99:         const modes = response.modes;
100:         const availableOptions = Array.isArray(modes.availableModes)
101:           ? modes.availableModes.map((m) => ({
102:               value: m.id,
103:               name: m.name || m.id,
104:               description: m.description,
105:             }))
106:           : [];
107: 
108:         result.modeState = {
109:           currentModeId: modes.currentModeId || availableOptions[0]?.value || "",
110:           availableModes: availableOptions,
111:           optionId: "mode",
112:         };
113:       }
114:     }
115: 
116:     return result;
117:   }

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 00:49:00)

Now I have a clear picture of how the session system works. Let me think through the problem:

**Current Architecture:**

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                      mimo-platform (Hono/Bun)                    │
│                                                                   │
│   ┌──────────────┐    ┌──────────────┐    ┌──────────────┐     │
│   │   Session    │───▶│    Agent     │───▶│  WebSocket   │     │
│   │ Repository   │    │   Service    │    │  Connection  │     │
│   └──────────────┘    └──────────────┘    └──────┬───────┘     │
│                                                  │               │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────┼───────────────┘
                                                   │ WebSocket
                                                   ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                      mimo-agent (Node.js)                        │
│                                                                   │
│   ┌──────────────┐    ┌──────────────┐    ┌──────────────┐     │
│   │   Session    │───▶│   AcpClient  │───▶│  Opencode    │     │
│   │   Manager    │    │              │    │   ACP Proc   │     │
│   └──────────────┘    └──────────────┘    └──────────────┘     │
│                                                                   │
│   Sessions: Map<sessionId, SessionInfo> (in-memory only)        │
│   AcpClients: Map<sessionId, AcpClient> (in-memory only)        │
│                                                                   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**The Problem:**
- When mimo-agent restarts, all sessions are lost because they exist only in-memory
- The session history (chat.jsonl) is persisted, but the ACP session ID is NOT
- When mimo-agent reconnects, it receives sessions via `session_ready` message
- But each session gets a NEW ACP session via `connection.newSession()`


- I see the core issue now. When the agent restarts, we lose the critical ACP session context. The `acpSessionId` exists temporarily in the session manager, but vanishes on restart. This breaks session continuity and requires rebuilding the entire conversation state from scratch.

The fundamental problem is the lack of a persistent mechanism to maintain the ACP session connection across process restarts. We need a way to serialize and restore the session state that bridges the gap between the platform and agent. The core issue involves maintaining session continuity across agent restarts. When the agent disconnects and reconnects, the platform has the session context, but the agent lacks the critical ACP session identifier. This forces a complete session reinitialization, breaking the conversation flow. Preserving the ACP session ID becomes crucial for seamless session persistence and recovery. The key challenge involves maintaining session continuity across agent restarts. When mimo-agent disconnects and reconnects, the platform must transfer critical session context to ensure seamless conversation recovery. Currently, the session initialization process loses critical ACP session information, preventing smooth session resumption. The proposed solution requires enhancing the session readiness mechanism to include the ACP session ID, enabling the agent to reconstruct its previous state accurately.

The recommended approach involves modifying the platform's agent initialization to preserve and transmit the ACP session identifier, which will allow the agent to reconstruct its previous conversational state upon reconnection. The platform faces a critical gap: it lacks visibility into the internal ACP session ID managed by mimo-agent. The session is created within the agent's AcpClient, but this information isn't communicated back to the platform. 

Potential solutions emerge: either the agent reports the ACP session ID after initialization, or the platform assumes responsibility for ACP session management. Both approaches require carefully redesigning the communication protocol between components to ensure session continuity and proper state synchronization.

The core challenge involves creating a robust mechanism to track and restore ACP session contexts across process restarts, ensuring seamless conversation continuity for users.
## Agent (2026-04-07 00:49:14)

This is a fascinating architectural challenge. Let me visualize the current session flow and the disconnect:

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  Current Session Lifecycle (The Problem)                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

mimo-platform                    mimo-agent                      ACP/opencode
     │                               │                                │
     │ 1. Create session (persisted) │                                │
     │──────────────────────────────▶│                                │
     │                               │                                │
     │ 2. Assign to agent            │                                │
     │────(WebSocket)───────────────▶│                                │
     │    sessions: [{sessionId}]    │                                │
     │                               │                                │
     │                               │ 3. NEW ACP session             │
     │                               │────────────newSession()───────▶│
     │                               │     returns acpSessionId         │
     │                               │◀───────────────────────────────│
     │                               │                                │
     │ 4. Chat history persisted     │                                │
     │    (chat.jsonl) ─────────────▶│                                │
     │                               │ 5. Prompts use acpSessionId    │
     │                               │                                │
     ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     │        AGENT RESTARTS (process crash/restart)                  │
     ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     │                               │                                │
     │ 6. Reconnect                  │                                │
     │────(WebSocket)───────────────▶│ 7. NEW ACP session (LOST!)     │
     │    sessions: [{sessionId}]    │────────────newSession()───────▶│
     │                               │     different acpSessionId       │
     │                               │◀───────────────────────────────│
     │                               │                                │
     ═══  ❌ ACP Session Context LOST ═══════════════════════════════════
     
     • Chat history exists (chat.jsonl)
     • Session exists (session.yaml)
     • But ACP conversation context is GONE
```

The core insight: **ACP sessions are stateful**. When opencode creates a session, it maintains conversation history, context window, system prompts, etc. When mimo-agent restarts and calls `newSession()`, it gets a *brand new* ACP session with no context.

## Key Questions to Explore

**1. Who should own the ACP session ID?**

Currently:
- ACP session is created inside mimo-agent's `AcpClient.initialize()`
- The ID (`acpSessionId`) lives only in mimo-agent memory
- mimo-platform knows nothing about it

Options:
- **A**: Store `acpSessionId` in mimo-platform (persisted to session.yaml)
- **B**: Store `acpSessionId` in a separate agent-side persistence
- **C**: Make ACP session ID deterministic based on mimo session ID

**2. How does ACP session resumption work?**

Let me check what the ACP protocol supports...

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 00:49:41)

The ACP SDK is installed. The key insight is in the `AcpClient.initialize()` method:

```typescript
const sessionResponse = await connection.newSession({
  cwd,
  mcpServers: [],
});
```

This creates a NEW session every time. Looking at the SDK, I need to understand if there's a way to:
1. Pass an existing session ID to resume/connect to it
2. Or if ACP sessions can be named/deterministic

### Tool Call [completed]: Check ACP SDK type definitions

**Tool:** execute
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 00:49:44
**Description:** Check ACP SDK type definitions
**Command:** cat /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-agent/node_modules/@agentclientprotocol/sdk/dist/*.d.ts 2>/dev/null | head -200 || echo "Checking for TypeScript definitions..."

````
import * as schema from "./schema/index.js";
export type * from "./schema/types.gen.js";
export * from "./schema/index.js";
export * from "./stream.js";
import type { Stream } from "./stream.js";
import type { Result, ErrorResponse, RequestHandler, NotificationHandler } from "./jsonrpc.js";
/**
 * An agent-side connection to a client.
 *
 * This class provides the agent's view of an ACP connection, allowing
 * agents to communicate with clients. It implements the {@link Client} interface
 * to provide methods for requesting permissions, accessing the file system,
 * and sending session updates.
 *
 * See protocol docs: [Agent](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/overview#agent)
 */
export declare class AgentSideConnection {
    #private;
    /**
     * Creates a new agent-side connection to a client.
     *
     * This establishes the communication channel from the agent's perspective
     * following the ACP specification.
     *
     * @param toAgent - A function that creates an Agent handler to process incoming client requests
     * @param stream - The bidirectional message stream for communication. Typically created using
     *                 {@link ndJsonStream} for stdio-based connections.
     *
     * See protocol docs: [Communication Model](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/overview#communication-model)
     */
    constructor(toAgent: (conn: AgentSideConnection) => Agent, stream: Stream);
    /**
     * Handles session update notifications from the agent.
     *
     * This is a notification endpoint (no response expected) that sends
     * real-time updates about session progress, including message chunks,
     * tool calls, and execution plans.
     *
     * Note: Clients SHOULD continue accepting tool call updates even after
     * sending a `session/cancel` notification, as the agent may send final
     * updates before responding with the cancelled stop reason.
     *
     * See protocol docs: [Agent Reports Output](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/prompt-turn#3-agent-reports-output)
     */
    sessionUpdate(params: schema.SessionNotification): Promise<void>;
    /**
     * Requests permission from the user for a tool call operation.
     *
     * Called by the agent when it needs user authorization before executing
     * a potentially sensitive operation. The client should present the options
     * to the user and return their decision.
     *
     * If the client cancels the prompt turn via `session/cancel`, it MUST
     * respond to this request with `RequestPermissionOutcome::Cancelled`.
     *
     * See protocol docs: [Requesting Permission](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/tool-calls#requesting-permission)
     */
    requestPermission(params: schema.RequestPermissionRequest): Promise<schema.RequestPermissionResponse>;
    /**
     * Reads content from a text file in the client's file system.
     *
     * Only available if the client advertises the `fs.readTextFile` capability.
     * Allows the agent to access file contents within the client's environment.
     *
     * See protocol docs: [Client](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/overview#client)
     */
    readTextFile(params: schema.ReadTextFileRequest): Promise<schema.ReadTextFileResponse>;
    /**
     * Writes content to a text file in the client's file system.
     *
     * Only available if the client advertises the `fs.writeTextFile` capability.
     * Allows the agent to create or modify files within the client's environment.
     *
     * See protocol docs: [Client](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/overview#client)
     */
    writeTextFile(params: schema.WriteTextFileRequest): Promise<schema.WriteTextFileResponse>;
    /**
     * Executes a command in a new terminal.
     *
     * Returns a `TerminalHandle` that can be used to get output, wait for exit,
     * kill the command, or release the terminal.
     *
     * The terminal can also be embedded in tool calls by using its ID in
     * `ToolCallContent` with type "terminal".
     *
     * @param params - The terminal creation parameters
     * @returns A handle to control and monitor the terminal
     */
    createTerminal(params: schema.CreateTerminalRequest): Promise<TerminalHandle>;
    /**
     * Extension method
     *
     * Allows the Agent to send an arbitrary request that is not part of the ACP spec.
     */
    extMethod(method: string, params: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<Record<string, unknown>>;
    /**
     * Extension notification
     *
     * Allows the Agent to send an arbitrary notification that is not part of the ACP spec.
     */
    extNotification(method: string, params: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<void>;
    /**
     * AbortSignal that aborts when the connection closes.
     *
     * This signal can be used to:
     * - Listen for connection closure: `connection.signal.addEventListener('abort', () => {...})`
     * - Check connection status synchronously: `if (connection.signal.aborted) {...}`
     * - Pass to other APIs (fetch, setTimeout) for automatic cancellation
     *
     * The connection closes when the underlying stream ends, either normally or due to an error.
     *
     * @example
     * ```typescript
     * const connection = new AgentSideConnection(agent, stream);
     *
     * // Listen for closure
     * connection.signal.addEventListener('abort', () => {
     *   console.log('Connection closed - performing cleanup');
     * });
     *
     * // Check status
     * if (connection.signal.aborted) {
     *   console.log('Connection is already closed');
     * }
     *
     * // Pass to other APIs
     * fetch(url, { signal: connection.signal });
     * ```
     */
    get signal(): AbortSignal;
    /**
     * Promise that resolves when the connection closes.
     *
     * The connection closes when the underlying stream ends, either normally or due to an error.
     * Once closed, the connection cannot send or receive any more messages.
     *
     * This is useful for async/await style cleanup:
     *
     * @example
     * ```typescript
     * const connection = new AgentSideConnection(agent, stream);
     * await connection.closed;
     * console.log('Connection closed - performing cleanup');
     * ```
     */
    get closed(): Promise<void>;
}
/**
 * Handle for controlling and monitoring a terminal created via `createTerminal`.
 *
 * Provides methods to:
 * - Get current output without waiting
 * - Wait for command completion
 * - Kill the running command
 * - Release terminal resources
 *
 * **Important:** Always call `release()` when done with the terminal to free resources.

 * The terminal supports async disposal via `Symbol.asyncDispose` for automatic cleanup.

 * You can use `await using` to ensure the terminal is automatically released when it
 * goes out of scope.
 */
export declare class TerminalHandle {
    #private;
    id: string;
    constructor(id: string, sessionId: string, conn: Connection);
    /**
     * Gets the current terminal output without waiting for the command to exit.
     */
    currentOutput(): Promise<schema.TerminalOutputResponse>;
    /**
     * Waits for the terminal command to complete and returns its exit status.
     */
    waitForExit(): Promise<schema.WaitForTerminalExitResponse>;
    /**
     * Kills the terminal command without releasing the terminal.
     *
     * The terminal remains valid after killing, allowing you to:
     * - Get the final output with `currentOutput()`
     * - Check the exit status
     * - Release the terminal when done
     *
     * Useful for implementing timeouts or cancellation.
     */
    kill(): Promise<schema.KillTerminalResponse>;
    /**
     * Releases the terminal and frees all associated resources.
     *
     * If the command is still running, it will be killed.
     * After release, the terminal ID becomes invalid and cannot be used
     * with other terminal methods.
     *
     * Tool calls that already reference this terminal will continue to
     * display its output.
     *
     * **Important:** Always call this method when done with the terminal.
     */
    release(): Promise<schema.ReleaseTerminalResponse | void>;
    [Symbol.asyncDispose](): Promise<void>;
````
