```
newSession(params: schema.NewSessionRequest): Promise<schema.NewSessionResponse>;
    /**
     * Loads an existing session to resume a previous conversation.
     *
     * This method is only available if the agent advertises the `loadSession` capability.
     *
     * The agent should:
     * - Restore the session context and conversation history
     * - Connect to the specified MCP servers
     * - Stream the entire conversation history back to the client via notifications
     *
     * The request may include `additionalDirectories` to set the complete list of
     * additional workspace roots for the loaded session.
     *
     * See protocol docs: [Loading Sessions](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/session-setup#loading-sessions)
     */
    loadSession(params: schema.LoadSessionRequest): Promise<schema.LoadSessionResponse>;
    /**
     * **UNSTABLE**
     *
     * This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
--
     * `newSession` without receiving an `auth_required` error.
     *
     * See protocol docs: [Initialization](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/initialization)
     */
    authenticate(params: schema.AuthenticateRequest): Promise<schema.AuthenticateResponse>;
    /**
     * Terminates the current authenticated session.
     *
     * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
     *
     * @experimental
     */
    unstable_logout(params: schema.LogoutRequest): Promise<schema.LogoutResponse>;
    /**
     * Processes a user prompt within a session.
     *
     * This method handles the whole lifecycle of a prompt:
     * - Receives user messages with optional context (files, images, etc.)
     * - Processes the prompt using language models
     * - Reports language model content and tool calls to the Clients
     * - Requests permission to run tools
--
    newSession(params: schema.NewSessionRequest): Promise<schema.NewSessionResponse>;
    /**
     * Loads an existing session to resume a previous conversation.
     *
     * This method is only available if the agent advertises the `loadSession` capability.
     *
     * The agent should:
     * - Restore the session context and conversation history
     * - Connect to the specified MCP servers
     * - Stream the entire conversation history back to the client via notifications
     *
     * The request may include `additionalDirectories` to set the complete list of
     * additional workspace roots for the loaded session.
     *
     * See protocol docs: [Loading Sessions](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/session-setup#loading-sessions)
     */
    loadSession?(params: schema.LoadSessionRequest): Promise<schema.LoadSessionResponse>;
    /**
     * **UNSTABLE**
     *
     * This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
--
     * `newSession` without receiving an `auth_required` error.
     *
     * See protocol docs: [Initialization](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/initialization)
     */
    authenticate(params: schema.AuthenticateRequest): Promise<schema.AuthenticateResponse | void>;
    /**
     * Terminates the current authenticated session.
     *
     * **UNSTABLE**: This capability is not part of the spec yet, and may be removed or changed at any point.
     *
     * @experimental
     */
    unstable_logout?(params: schema.LogoutRequest): Promise<schema.LogoutResponse | void>;

     * @experimental
     */
    additionalDirectories?: Array<string>;
    /**
     * The working directory for this session.
     */
    cwd: string;
    /**
     * List of MCP servers to connect to for this session.
     */
    mcpServers: Array<McpServer>;
    /**
     * The ID of the session to load.
     */
    sessionId: SessionId;
};
/**
 * Response from loading an existing session.
 */
export type LoadSessionResponse = {
    /**
     * The _meta property is reserved by ACP to allow clients and agents to attach additional
     * metadata to their interactions. Implementations MUST NOT make assumptions about values at
     * these keys.
     *
     * See protocol docs: [Extensibility](https://agentclientprotocol.com/protocol/extensibility)
     */
    _meta?: {
        [key: string]: unknown;
```
## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 00:50:07)

**Perfect!** Now I have the full picture. The ACP protocol has a `loadSession` method that's specifically designed for resuming existing sessions. It takes a `sessionId` and restores the conversation context.

#### The Solution Design

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  Proposed Solution: Persistent ACP Session Binding                        │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

mimo-platform                     mimo-agent                       ACP/opencode
     │                                │                                │
     │  1. Create Mimo session        │                                │
     │  (persisted to session.yaml)   │                                │
     │                                 │                                │
     │  2. Assign to agent            │                                │
     │────(WebSocket)─────────────────▶│                                │
     │     sessions: [{sessionId}]    │  3. Call newSession()         │
     │                                │───────────────────────────────▶│
     │                                │     returns acpSessionId       │
     │                                │◀───────────────────────────────│
     │  4. Store acpSessionId         │  5. Store acpSessionId locally │
     │────save_acp_session────────────▶│     (for recovery)            │
     │     {sessionId, acpSessionId}   │                                │
     │◄───────────────────────────────│                                │
     │                                │                                │
     │  6. Chat flows...              │  7. ACP prompts use acpSessionId│
     │                                │                                │
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     │                    AGENT RESTARTS                                   │
     ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
     │                                │  8. Read local cache            │
     │                                │     {sessionId, acpSessionId}   │
     │                                │                                │
     │  9. Reconnect                  │                                │
     │────(WebSocket)─────────────────▶│                                │
     │     sessions: [{sessionId}]    │ 10. Check: have acpSessionId?  │
     │                                │     YES → Call loadSession()     │
     │                                │────────loadSession({sessionId})─▶│
     │                                │     Resume existing ACP session │
     │                                │◀───────────────────────────────│
     │                                │     NO → Call newSession()      │
     │                                │     (fallback for new sessions) │
     │                                │                                │
     ═══  ✅ ACP Session Context PRESERVED ════════════════════════════════════
```

#### Implementation Strategy

**Key insight**: The ACP `sessionId` parameter in `loadSession()` is what we need to persist. When mimo-agent restarts, it should:

1. **Check its local cache** (simple JSON file) for `{mimoSessionId: acpSessionId}` mappings
2. **If found**: Call `loadSession({ sessionId: acpSessionId, cwd, mcpServers })` instead of `newSession()`
3. **If not found**: Fall back to `newSession()` (new session scenario)

**Why local cache in mimo-agent?**
- The agent is the one directly communicating with ACP
- WebSocket reconnect happens after agent restart
- Platform shouldn't need to know ACP internals
- Cache is scoped to agent's filesystem (`~/.mimo/agents/{agentId}/acp-sessions.json`)

**Why not store in session.yaml?**
- session.yaml is managed by mimo-platform
- ACP session ID is an implementation detail of the agent
- Avoids tight coupling between platform and ACP specifics

**What about the chat history?**
- Mimo-platform already persists chat to `chat.jsonl`
- ACP's `loadSession` restores the LLM's internal context (system prompt, conversation history, tool state)
- Both work together: ACP context + Mimo chat history = full continuity

#### Open Questions

1. **Does opencode support `loadSession`?**
   - Need to check if it advertises the `loadSession` capability
   
2. **What happens to in-flight prompts during restart?**
   - They'll fail, client should retry
   
3. **Session expiration?**
   - ACP sessions may expire server-side
   - Need fallback to `newSession()` if `loadSession` fails

## Next Steps

This feels like a solid direction. Want me to:

1. **Dive deeper** into opencode's ACP capabilities?
2. **Explore edge cases** (what if session expired, what if chat.jsonl diverges from ACP history)?
3. **Design the persistence format** (where/how to store the mapping)?
4. **Start a formal change** with `/opsx:new` to capture this design?

What resonates with you? Any concerns about this approach?## User (2026-04-07 00:50:31)

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 00:50:32)

The user wants me to continue the exploration. Let me summarize what I've learned and think through the solution.

**Key Findings:**

1. **The Problem:**
   - ACP sessions are stateful (conversation history, context window, etc.)
   - When mimo-agent restarts, it calls `newSession()` again
   - This creates a *brand new* ACP session with no prior context
   - The old ACP session ID is lost

2. **The Solution:**
   - ACP protocol has a `loadSession` method specifically for resuming sessions!
   - `LoadSessionRequest` takes a `sessionId` parameter
   - The agent should restore conversation history and context

3. **Current Architecture:**
   - `AcpClient` in mimo-agent has a `session` property containing `acpSessionId`
   - This is NOT persisted anywhere
   - When agent restarts, it creates new `AcpClient` and calls `newSession()`

**The Approach:**

The cleanest solution is:
1. When `AcpClient` creates a session via `newSession()`, capture the `acpSessionId`
2. Send this `acpSessionId` back to mimo-platform
3. mimo-platform stores it in session.yaml (persisted)
4. When agent reconnects, mimo-platform sends the stored `acpSessionId`
5. Agent uses `loadSession()` instead of `newSession()` if `acpSessionId` exists

**Architecture Visualization:**

```

     │   - acpSessionId: null          │                                │
     │                               │                                │

**Implementation Steps:**

1. **Add acpSessionId to Session type** (mimo-platform)
2. **Send acpSessionId on session_ready** (mimo-platform)
3. **Receive acp_session_created event** (mimo-platform) - store acpSessionId
4. **Modify AcpClient** (mimo-agent):
   - Accept optional `acpSessionId` in constructor
   - Use `loadSession()` instead of `newSession()` if `acpSessionId` exists
5. **Send acp_session_created after newSession** (mimo-agent)
6. **Handle acpSessionId in spawnAcpProcess** (mimo-agent)

This is a solid design. The key insight is that ACP already has `loadSession()` - we just need to wire it up properly and persist the ACP session ID in mimo-platform.

     ═══  ✅ ACP Session Context PRESERVED ═══════════════════════════════

## The Discovery

The ACP protocol already has a **`loadSession`** method specifically for resuming sessions! From the SDK docs:

> "Loads an existing session to resume a previous conversation... The agent should restore the session context and conversation history."

**`LoadSessionRequest`** requires:
- `sessionId: SessionId` - the ACP session ID to resume
- `cwd: string` - working directory
- `mcpServers: Array<McpServer>` - MCP servers

## The Solution

### Current Gap
- `AcpClient` stores `acpSessionId` in memory only (line 92 in `client.ts`)
- When mimo-agent restarts, it creates a fresh `AcpClient` and calls `newSession()`
- The previous ACP session is orphaned

##### The Fix
1. **Persist `acpSessionId` in mimo-platform** (in `session.yaml`)
2. **Send `acpSessionId` to agent** on `session_ready` message
3. **Agent reports back** `acpSessionId` after creating session (`acp_session_created` event)
4. **On reconnect**, if `acpSessionId` exists, call **`loadSession()`** instead of `newSession()`

## Key Design Decisions

| Decision | Rationale |
|----------|-----------|
| Store `acpSessionId` in session.yaml | Session is the natural owner; survives agent restarts |
| Platform owns persistence | Agent is stateless/ephemeral; platform is the source of truth |
| Use `loadSession` vs `newSession` | ACP-native resumption; restores full context |

#### Questions to Consider

1. **What if ACP session is expired/invalid?** → Fallback to `newSession()`, clear `acpSessionId`
2. **Multiple agents per session?** → Each would share the same `acpSessionId` (probably fine)
3. **Manual session clearing?** → User could "Reset ACP Session" to force fresh context

Does this approach resonate? Want me to create an OpenSpec change for this? (That would involve exiting explore mode with `/opsx:new acp-session-resumption` or `/opsx:ff acp-session-resumption` to fast-forward through artifacts)

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 00:53:54)

The user is clarifying their preferences:

1. "just do nothing, for now" - If ACP session is expired/invalid, just create a new one. No complex fallback logic.
2. "yes but not will happen" - Multiple agents per session is not a concern (won't happen)
3. "yes but only Reset Session" - Manual clearing should be done via "Reset Session" feature. This adds a message to the chat history indicating when it was cleared, but mimo-platform's chat history is preserved (we're only resetting the ACP side).

So the refined approach:
- When agent restarts and has `acpSessionId`, try `loadSession()`
- If it fails/expired, just call `newSession()` and get a fresh session
- "Reset Session" is a user-initiated action that:
  - Calls something like `acpClient.resetSession()` or terminates and recreates with `newSession()`
  - Adds a system message to chat.jsonl: "Session reset at {timestamp}"
  - Updates the persisted `acpSessionId` to the new one

This is good thinking. Let me summarize the approach and offer to capture it in an OpenSpec change.
## Agent (2026-04-07 00:54:01)

Got it. So the approach simplifies to:

**Minimal Fallback**: Try `loadSession()` with persisted ID, if it fails for any reason → just `newSession()` and move on. No complex error handling.

**Single Agent**: One agent per session, no concurrency concerns.

**Reset Flow**: User clicks "Reset Session" → agent gets `reset_session` message → terminates ACP → `newSession()` → reports new ID → platform updates `session.yaml` AND appends system message to `chat.jsonl`.

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 00:55:12)

Hmm, the user is bringing up an important point - if multiple ACP processes can be spawned for a single mimo-platform session (like when handling multiple prompts or canceling/restarting), we need to be careful about session mapping. Let me think about this...

Looking at the code I read:
1. In `mimo-agent/src/index.ts`, when a user sends a message, it calls `spawnAcpProcess()` which creates a NEW ACP session via `acpClient.initialize()` which calls `connection.newSession()`
2. Each call to `spawnAcpProcess()` creates a fresh ACP process and fresh ACP session
3. The `acpSessionId` is stored in the `AcpClient` instance, which is stored in `this.acpClients` map keyed by `sessionId`

So actually, there might be multiple ACP sessions over the lifetime of one mimo-platform session, but only ONE at a time (the current active one).

But wait - looking more carefully at `handleAcpRequest`:
```typescript
private handleAcpRequest(message: any): void {
  const sessionId = message.sessionId;
  // ...
  console.log(`[mimo-agent] Restarting ACP for session ${sessionId}`);
  this.spawnAcpProcess(session);
}
```

And `handleCancelRequest`:
```typescript
if (session.acpProcess) {
  session.acpProcess.kill("SIGTERM");
  this.sessionManager.setSessionAcpProcess(sessionId, null);
  this.acpClients.delete(sessionId);
}
```

So the pattern is:
- When a request comes in, spawn a new ACP process (which creates new ACP session)
- When cancel is called, kill the process and remove the client


- Each new prompt spawns a fresh ACP session, potentially creating multiple sessions over time
- The critical insight is that each ACP session is temporary and tied to a specific request or prompt

I see now that the session management is more dynamic than initially assumed. Each interaction spawns a new, isolated ACP session that gets cleaned up after use. This means the session mapping needs to handle multiple transient ACP sessions per platform session.
## Agent (2026-04-07 00:55:18)

Wait, you're right - I need to look closer at the lifecycle. Let me trace through what actually happens:

```
User sends message
    ↓
platform → agent: {type: "acp_request", sessionId}
    ↓
agent: spawnAcpProcess(session)
    → spawn opencode process
    → new ACP session (acpSessionId)
    → store in acpClients[sessionId]
    → handle prompt
    → ACP process exits
    → acpClients.delete(sessionId)
```

And `handleCancelRequest`:
```
{type: "cancel_request", sessionId}
    ↓
agent: kill acpProcess
    → acpClients.delete(sessionId)
```

So actually... **each prompt creates a fresh ACP session**. The `acpSessionId` is ephemeral - it lives only for the duration of one prompt/response cycle.

```
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  Current Reality: Multiple ACP Sessions Per Platform Session   │

│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘     │
│                                                                  │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

So the ACP session is **NOT** long-lived. Each prompt gets a fresh ACP session, and ACP's context window only contains the messages sent in THAT session.

<type>file</type>
<content>1: import { join } from "path";
2: import { existsSync, mkdirSync, appendFileSync, readFileSync } from "fs";
3: import { getPaths } from "../config/paths.js";
4: 
5: export interface ChatMessage {
6:   role: "user" | "assistant" | "system";
7:   content: string;
8:   timestamp: string;
9:   metadata?: Record<string, unknown>;
10: }
11: 
12: export class ChatService {
13:   private getChatPath(sessionId: string): string {
14:     // Store chat in the session directory
15:     const Paths = getPaths();
16:     const sessionDir = this.findSessionDir(sessionId);
17:     if (!sessionDir) {
18:       throw new Error(`Session ${sessionId} not found`);
19:     }
20:     return join(sessionDir, "chat.jsonl");
21:   }
22: 
23:   private findSessionDir(sessionId: string): string | null {
24:     const Paths = getPaths();
25:     if (!existsSync(Paths.projects)) {
26:       return null;
27:     }
28: 
29:     const { readdirSync } = require("fs");
30:     const projectEntries = readdirSync(Paths.projects, { withFileTypes: true });
31:     
32:     for (const projectEntry of projectEntries) {
33:       if (projectEntry.isDirectory()) {
34:         const sessionsDir = join(Paths.projects, projectEntry.name, "sessions");
35:         if (existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
36:           const sessionDir = join(sessionsDir, sessionId);
37:           if (existsSync(sessionDir)) {
38:             return sessionDir;
39:           }
40:         }
41:       }
42:     }
43: 
44:     return null;
45:   }
46: 
47:   async saveMessage(sessionId: string, message: ChatMessage): Promise<void> {
48:     const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
49:     const line = JSON.stringify(message) + "\n";
50:     appendFileSync(chatPath, line, "utf-8");
51:   }
52: 
53:   async loadHistory(sessionId: string): Promise<ChatMessage[]> {
54:     try {
55:       const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
56:       if (!existsSync(chatPath)) {
57:         return [];
58:       }
59: 
60:       const content = readFileSync(chatPath, "utf-8");
61:       const lines = content.trim().split("\n").filter(line => line);
62:       
63:       return lines.map((line) => JSON.parse(line) as ChatMessage);
64:     } catch {
65:       return [];
66:     }
67:   }
68: 
69:   async appendToHistory(sessionId: string, messages: ChatMessage[]): Promise<void> {
70:     const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
71:     const lines = messages.map((msg) => JSON.stringify(msg)).join("\n") + "\n";
72:     appendFileSync(chatPath, lines, "utf-8");
73:   }
74: 
75:   async clearHistory(sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
76:     const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
77:     if (existsSync(chatPath)) {
78:       const { unlinkSync } = require("fs");
79:       unlinkSync(chatPath);
80:     }
81:   }
82: }
83: 
84: export const chatService = new ChatService();

43:     const wsUrl = `${window.location.protocol === 'https:' ? 'wss:' : 'ws:'}//${window.location.host}/ws/chat/${sessionId}`;
44:     
45:     chatSocket = new WebSocket(wsUrl);
46:     
47:     chatSocket.onopen = () => {
48:       console.log('Chat WebSocket connected');
49:       showConnectionStatus('connected');
50:       
51:       // Request current state from agent

53:         type: 'request_state',
54:         sessionId: currentSessionId,
55:       }));
56:     };

58:     chatSocket.onmessage = (event) => {
59:       const data = JSON.parse(event.data);
60:       handleWebSocketMessage(data);
61:     };
62:     
63:     chatSocket.onclose = () => {
64:       console.log('Chat WebSocket disconnected');
65:       showConnectionStatus('disconnected');
66:       
67:       // Attempt reconnect after 3 seconds
68:       setTimeout(() => {
69:         if (currentSessionId) {
70:           connectWebSocket(currentSessionId);
71:         }
72:       }, 3000);
73:     };
74:

78:     };

81:   // Handle incoming WebSocket messages
82:   function handleWebSocketMessage(data) {
83:     console.log('[CHAT] Received message type:', data.type, data);
84:     
85:     switch (data.type) {
86:       case 'thought_start':
87:         startThoughtSection();
88:         break;
89:         
90:       case 'thought_chunk':
91:         appendThoughtChunk(data.content);
92:         break;
93:         
94:       case 'thought_end':
95:         endThoughtSection();
96:         break;
97:         
98:       case 'message_chunk':
99:         appendMessageChunk(data.content);
100:         break;
101:         
102:       case 'usage_update':
103:         updateUsageDisplay(data.usage);
104:         endMessageStream();
105:         break;
106:         
107:       case 'message':
108:         // Check if this is a user message we already added locally
109:         if (data.role === 'user' && pendingUserMessages.has(data.content)) {
110:           pendingUserMessages.delete(data.content);
111:           return; // Skip - already added locally
112:         }
113:         addMessageToChat(data);
114:         break;
115:         
116:       case 'error':
117:         showError(data.message);
118:         break;
119:         
120:       case 'history':
121:         loadChatHistory(data.messages);
122:         break;
123: 
124:       case 'session_initialized':
125:         // Initialize model and mode selectors
126:         console.log('[INIT] session_initialized received:', data);
127:         if (data.modelState) {
128:           updateModelSelector(data.modelState);
129:         } else {
130:           console.log('[INIT] No modelState in message');
131:         }
132:         if (data.modeState) {
133:           updateModeSelector(data.modeState);
134:         } else {
135:           console.log('[INIT] No modeState in message');
136:         }
137:         break;
138: 
139:       case 'model_state':
140:         // Update model selector
141:         if (data.modelState) {
142:           updateModelSelector(data.modelState);
143:         }
144:         break;
145: 
146:       case 'mode_state':
147:         // Update mode selector
148:         if (data.modeState) {
149:           updateModeSelector(data.modeState);
150:         }
151:         break;
152:     }
153:   }

157:     const chatForm = document.querySelector('#chat-form');
158:     const chatInput = document.querySelector('#chat-input');
159:

161:

164:       
165:       const message = chatInput.value.trim();
166:       if (!message) return;
167:       
168:       // Add user message immediately for better UX
169:       addMessageToChat({
170:         role: 'user',
171:         content: message,
172:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
173:       });
174:       
175:       // Track this message to prevent duplicate when server echoes it
176:       pendingUserMessages.add(message);
177:       
178:       // Clear input
179:       chatInput.value = '';
180:       
181:       // Send via WebSocket if connected
182:       if (chatSocket && chatSocket.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
183:         chatSocket.send(JSON.stringify({
184:           type: 'send_message',
185:           content: message,
186:         }));
187:       } else {
188:         // Fallback to HTTP
189:         sendMessageHttp(message);
190:       }
191:     });
192:   }

194:   // Send message via HTTP fallback
195:   async function sendMessageHttp(message) {
196:     try {
197:       const res = await fetch(`/sessions/${currentSessionId}/chat`, {
198:         method: 'POST',
199:         headers: {
200:           'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
201:         },
202:         body: new URLSearchParams({ message }).toString(),
203:       });
204:       
205:       if (!res.ok) {
206:         showError('Failed to send message');
207:       }
208:     } catch (error) {
209:       showError('Failed to send message: ' + error.message);
210:     }

383:   // Append a chunk to the thought section
384:   function appendThoughtChunk(text) {
385:     if (!currentThoughtContent) {
386:       // Thought section might not exist yet, create it
387:       startThoughtSection();
388:     }
389:     if (!currentThoughtContent) return;
390:     currentThoughtContent.textContent += text || '';
391:     scrollToBottom();
392:   }

395:   function endThoughtSection() {
396:     // Just clear the reference, the thought section stays in the message
397:     currentThoughtElement = null;
398:     currentThoughtContent = null;
399:   }
400: 
401:   // Append a chunk to the assistant message
402:   function appendMessageChunk(text) {
403:     if (!currentMessageElement) return; // Message should already exist from thought_start
404:     
405:     // Find or create a container for the response text (after thought section)
406:     let responseContent = currentMessageElement.querySelector('.message-response');
407:     if (!responseContent) {
408:       responseContent = document.createElement('div');
409:       responseContent.className = 'message-response';
410:       currentMessageElement.querySelector('.message-content')?.appendChild(responseContent);
411:     }
412:     
413:     // Remove cursor if exists
414:     const existingCursor = responseContent.querySelector('.typing-cursor');
415:     if (existingCursor) {
416:       existingCursor.remove();
417:     }
418:     
419:     // Append text
420:     responseContent.textContent += text;
421:     
422:     // Add blinking cursor at end
423:     const cursor = document.createElement('span');
424:     cursor.className = 'typing-cursor';
425:     cursor.textContent = '▋';
426:     cursor.style.color = '#51cf66';
427:     cursor.style.animation = 'blink 1s infinite';
428:     responseContent.appendChild(cursor);
429:     
430:     scrollToBottom();
431:   }
432: 
433:   // End the message stream
434:   function endMessageStream() {
435:     if (!currentMessageElement) return;
436:     
437:     // Remove streaming indicator
438:     const indicator = currentMessageElement.querySelector('.streaming-indicator');
439:     if (indicator) {
440:       indicator.remove();
441:     }
442:     
443:     // Remove typing cursor
444:     const responseContent = currentMessageElement.querySelector('.message-response');
445:     if (responseContent) {
446:       const cursor = responseContent.querySelector('.typing-cursor');
447:       if (cursor) {
448:         cursor.remove();
449:       }
450:     }
451:     
452:     currentMessageElement.classList.remove('streaming');
453:     currentMessageElement = null;
454:     currentMessageContent = null;
455:     currentThoughtElement = null;
456:     currentThoughtContent = null;
457:   }

459:   // Update usage display
460:   function updateUsageDisplay(usage) {
461:     const usageEl = document.querySelector('#chat-usage');
462:     if (!usageEl) return;
463:     
464:     if (!usage) {
465:       usageEl.textContent = '';
466:       usageEl.style.display = 'none';
467:       return;
468:     }
469:     
470:     const parts = [];
471:     
472:     // Show cost if available
473:     if (usage.cost?.amount !== undefined) {
474:       const amount = usage.cost.amount / 100;
475:       parts.push(`Cost: $${amount.toFixed(4)}`);
476:     }
477:     
478:     // Show tokens used if available
479:     if (usage.used !== undefined) {
480:       parts.push(`Tokens: ${usage.used.toLocaleString()}`);
481:     }
482:     
483:     // Show context size if available
484:     if (usage.size !== undefined) {
485:       parts.push(`Context: ${usage.size.toLocaleString()}`);
486:     }
487:     
488:     if (parts.length > 0) {
489:       usageEl.textContent = parts.join(' | ');
490:       usageEl.style.display = 'block';
491:     } else {
492:       usageEl.textContent = '';
493:       usageEl.style.display = 'none';
494:     }
495:   }
496:

499:     const chatContainer = document.querySelector('#chat-messages');
500:     if (chatContainer) {
501:       chatContainer.scrollTop = chatContainer.scrollHeight;
502:     }
503:   }

531: 
532:   // Load chat history
533:   function loadChatHistory(messages) {
534:     const chatContainer = document.querySelector('#chat-messages');
535:     if (!chatContainer) return;
536:     
537:     // Clear existing messages
538:     chatContainer.innerHTML = '';
539:     
540:     // Track current thought and message for grouping
541:     let currentThoughtText = '';
542:     let currentMessageText = '';
543:     let inThought = false;
544:     let inMessage = false;
545:     
546:     messages.forEach(msg => {
547:       // Skip available_commands_update in history
548:       if (msg.content && msg.content.includes('available_commands_update')) {
549:         return;
550:       }
551:       
552:       // Try to parse JSON content for assistant messages
553:       if (msg.role === 'assistant' && msg.content) {
554:         try {
555:           const parsed = JSON.parse(msg.content);
556:           if (parsed.update) {
557:             const updateType = parsed.update.sessionUpdate;
558:             const text = parsed.update.content?.text || '';
559:             
560:             // Handle thought chunks
561:             if (updateType === 'agent_thought_chunk') {
562:               if (!inThought) {
563:                 inThought = true;
564:                 currentThoughtText = '';
565:               }
566:               currentThoughtText += text;
567:               return; // Skip adding as individual message
568:             }
569:             
570:             // Handle message chunks
571:             if (updateType === 'agent_message_chunk') {
572:               if (inThought) {
573:                 // End thought section first
574:                 addThoughtToChat(chatContainer, currentThoughtText);
575:                 inThought = false;
576:                 currentThoughtText = '';
577:               }
578:               if (!inMessage) {
579:                 inMessage = true;
580:                 currentMessageText = '';
581:               }
582:               currentMessageText += text;
583:               return; // Skip adding as individual message
584:             }
585:             
586:             // Handle usage
587:             if (updateType === 'usage_update') {
588:               updateUsageDisplay(parsed.update.cost || {});
589:               return;
590:             }
591:             
592:             // Skip other types
593:             return;
594:           }
595:         } catch (e) {
596:           // Not JSON, display as-is
597:         }
598:       }
599:       
600:       // User message or unparseable content
601:       addMessageToChat(msg);
602:     });
603:     
604:     // Add any pending thought
605:     if (inThought && currentThoughtText) {
606:       addThoughtToChat(chatContainer, currentThoughtText);
607:     }
608:     
609:     // Add any pending message
610:     if (inMessage && currentMessageText) {
611:       addMessageToChat({
612:         role: 'assistant',
613:         content: currentMessageText,
614:       });
615:     }
616:     
617:     scrollToBottom();
618:   }
619: 
620:   // Add thought section to chat (legacy - for old ACP format)
621:   function addThoughtToChat(container, text) {
622:     if (!text || !text.trim()) return;
623:     
624:     const thoughtDiv = document.createElement('div');
625:     thoughtDiv.className = 'message message-thought';
626:     thoughtDiv.style.background = '#2d2d2d';
627:     thoughtDiv.style.borderRadius = '4px';
628:     
629:     const header = document.createElement('div');
630:     header.className = 'thought-header';
631:     header.innerHTML = '<span class="thought-toggle">▶</span> Thought Process';
632:     header.style.cursor = 'pointer';
633:     header.style.fontSize = '0.9em';
634:     header.style.padding = '4px 8px';
635:     header.style.background = '#3d3d3d';
636:     
637:     const content = document.createElement('div');
638:     content.className = 'thought-content';
639:     content.textContent = text;
640:     content.style.display = 'none';
641:     content.style.padding = '8px';
642:     content.style.fontSize = '0.9em';
643:     content.style.color = '#d4d4d4';
644:     content.style.background = '#2d2d2d';
645:     
646:     header.addEventListener('click', () => {
647:       const isVisible = content.style.display !== 'none';
648:       content.style.display = isVisible ? 'none' : 'block';
649:       header.querySelector('.thought-toggle').textContent = isVisible ? '▶' : '▼';
650:     });
651:     
652:     thoughtDiv.appendChild(header);
653:     thoughtDiv.appendChild(content);
654:     container.appendChild(thoughtDiv);
655:   }
656: 
657:   // Request chat replay
658:   function replayChat() {
659:     if (chatSocket && chatSocket.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
660:       chatSocket.send(JSON.stringify({
661:         type: 'request_replay',
662:       }));
663:     }
664:   }
665: 
666:   // Expose functions globally
667:   window.MIMO_CHAT = {
668:     init: initChat,
669:     send: (msg) => {
670:       if (chatSocket && chatSocket.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
671:         chatSocket.send(JSON.stringify({
672:           type: 'send_message',
673:           content: msg,
674:         }));
675:       }
676:     },
677:     replay: replayChat,

679:       if (chatSocket && chatSocket.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {

681:           type: 'set_model',

683:         }));
684:       }
685:     },

690:           modeId: modeId,
691:         }));
692:       }
693:     },
694:   };

696:   // Auto-initialize if session ID is available

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 00:55:42)

Now I see! Looking at line 181-190 and the HTTP fallback at line 195-211:

The frontend sends:
1. **WebSocket**: `type: 'send_message'` → goes to platform WebSocket handler
2. **HTTP fallback**: POST `/sessions/${currentSessionId}/chat` → HTTP endpoint

So messages go through the platform, not directly to the agent. Let me find where the platform forwards messages to the agent.

<content>1: /** @jsx jsx */
2: import { jsx } from "hono/jsx";
3: import { Hono } from "hono";

13: 
14: import { SessionDetailPage } from "../components/SessionDetailPage.js";
15: import { SessionCreatePage } from "../components/SessionCreatePage.js";
16: import { SessionListPage } from "../components/SessionListPage.js";
17: import { sessionStateService } from "./state.js";
18: import { fossilServerManager } from "../vcs/fossil-server.js";
19: import type { Context } from "hono";
20: 
21: const router = new Hono();
22: 
23: // Helper to get authenticated username from cookie
24: async function getAuthUsername(c: Context): Promise<string | null> {
25:   const cookieHeader = c.req.header("Cookie");
26:   const usernameMatch = cookieHeader?.match(/username=([^;]+)/);
27:   const username = usernameMatch ? usernameMatch[1] : null;
28:   if (username) return username;
29:   
30:   // Also check JWT token
31:   const tokenMatch = cookieHeader?.match(/token=([^;]+)/);
32:   const token = tokenMatch ? tokenMatch[1] : null;
33:   
34:   if (token) {
35:     const payload = await verifyToken(token);
36:     if (payload) return payload.username;
37:   }
38:   
39:   return null;
40: }
41: 
42: // Helper to get projectId from either URL param or query param
43: function getProjectId(c: Context): string | null {
44:   // Try URL param first (for nested routes)
45:   const projectId = c.req.param("projectId");
46:   if (projectId) return projectId;
47:   
48:   // Fall back to query param (for flat routes)
49:   return c.req.query("projectId");
50: }
51: 
52: // GET /sessions or /projects/:projectId/sessions - List sessions for a project
53: router.get("/", async (c: Context) => {
54:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
55:   if (!username) {
56:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
57:   }
58: 
59:   const projectId = getProjectId(c);
60:   if (!projectId) {
61:     return c.text("Project ID required", 400);
62:   }
63: 
64:   const project = await projectRepository.findById(projectId);
65:   if (!project || project.owner !== username) {
66:     return c.text("Project not found", 404);
67:   }
68: 
69:   const sessions = await sessionRepository.listByProject(projectId);
70: 
71:   return c.html(
72:     <SessionListPage project={project} sessions={sessions} />
73:   );
74: });
75: 
76: // GET /sessions/new or /projects/:projectId/sessions/new - Create session form
77: router.get("/new", async (c: Context) => {
78:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
79:   if (!username) {
80:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
81:   }
82: 
83:   const projectId = getProjectId(c);
84:   if (!projectId) {
85:     return c.text("Project ID required", 400);
86:   }
87: 
88:   const project = await projectRepository.findById(projectId);
89:   if (!project || project.owner !== username) {
90:     return c.text("Project not found", 404);
91:   }
92: 
93:   const agents = await agentService.listAgentsByOwner(username);
94: 
95:   return c.html(
96:     <SessionCreatePage project={project} agents={agents} />
97:   );
98: });
99: 
100: // POST /sessions or /projects/:projectId/sessions - Create new session
101: router.post("/", async (c: Context) => {
102:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
103:   if (!username) {
104:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
105:   }
106: 
107:   const body = await c.req.parseBody();
108:   const name = body.name as string;
109:   const projectId = (body.projectId as string) || getProjectId(c);
110:   const assignedAgentId = (body.assignedAgentId as string) || null;
111: 
112:   if (!name || !projectId) {
113:     return c.text("Name and project ID required", 400);
114:   }
115: 
116:   const project = await projectRepository.findById(projectId);
117:   if (!project || project.owner !== username) {
118:     return c.text("Project not found", 404);
119:   }
120: 
121:   // Create session with upstream and checkout directories
122:   const session = await sessionRepository.create({
123:     name: name as string,
124:     projectId: projectId as string,
125:     owner: username,
126:     assignedAgentId: assignedAgentId || undefined,
127:   });
128: 
129:   // Initialize repository: clone → import to fossil
130:   // Note: checkout is created by agent when it receives session_ready
131:   try {
132:     // Step 1: Clone repository to upstream/
133:     const cloneResult = await vcs.cloneRepository(
134:       project.repoUrl,
135:       project.repoType,
136:       session.upstreamPath,
137:       undefined,
138:       project.sourceBranch
139:     );
140:     
141:     if (!cloneResult.success) {
142:       await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
143:       return c.text(`Failed to clone repository: ${cloneResult.error}`, 500);
144:     }
145: 
146:     // Step 2: Import to fossil proxy (repo.fossil)
147:     const fossilPath = `${session.upstreamPath}/../repo.fossil`;
148:     const importResult = await vcs.importToFossil(
149:       session.upstreamPath,
150:       project.repoType,
151:       fossilPath
152:     );
153:     
154:     if (!importResult.success) {
155:       await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
156:       return c.text(`Failed to import to fossil: ${importResult.error}`, 500);
157:     }
158: 
159:     // Step 3: Create new branch if specified (after Fossil import is complete)
160:     if (project.newBranch) {
161:       const branchResult = await vcs.createBranch(
162:         project.newBranch,
163:         project.repoType,
164:         session.upstreamPath
165:       );
166:       if (!branchResult.success) {
167:         await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
168:         return c.text(`Failed to create branch '${project.newBranch}': ${branchResult.error}`, 500);
169:       }
170:     }
171: 
172:     // Step 4: Create fossil user for agent access
173:     const agentWorkspaceUser = `agent-${session.id.slice(0, 8)}`;
174:     const agentWorkspacePassword = crypto.randomUUID().replace(/-/g, "").slice(0, 16);
175:     const userResult = await vcs.createFossilUser(fossilPath, agentWorkspaceUser, agentWorkspacePassword);
176:     
177:     if (!userResult.success) {
178:       console.error("[session] Failed to create fossil user:", userResult.error);
179:       // Non-fatal - session can still work, just log the error
180:     }
181:     
182:     // Save credentials to session
183:     await sessionRepository.update(session.id, {
184:       agentWorkspaceUser,
185:       agentWorkspacePassword,
186:     });
187:     
188:     // Step 5: Open fossil checkout in agent-workspace
189:     const openResult = await vcs.openFossil(fossilPath, session.agentWorkspacePath);
190:     if (!openResult.success) {
191:       console.error("[session] Failed to open fossil in agent-workspace:", openResult.error);
192:       await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
193:       return c.text("Failed to open fossil checkout", 500);
194:     }
195:   } catch (error) {
196:     console.error("Failed to setup session:", error);
197:     await sessionRepository.delete(projectId, session.id);
198:     return c.text("Failed to setup session repository", 500);
199:   }
200: 
201:   return c.redirect(`/projects/${projectId}/sessions/${session.id}`);
202: });
203: 
204: // GET /sessions/:id or /projects/:projectId/sessions/:id - View session detail
205: router.get("/:id", async (c: Context) => {
206:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
207:   if (!username) {
208:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
209:   }
210: 
211:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
212:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
213:   
214:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
215:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
216:   }
217: 
218:   const project = await projectRepository.findById(session.projectId);
219:   if (!project) {
220:     return c.text("Project not found", 404);
221:   }
222: 
223:   // Get chat history
224:   const chatHistory = await chatService.loadHistory(sessionId);
225:   
226:   // Get assigned agent if any
227:   let agent = undefined;
228:   if (session.assignedAgentId) {
229:     agent = await agentRepository.findById(session.assignedAgentId);
230:   }
231: 
232:   // Get model/mode state from in-memory store
233:   const modelState = sessionStateService.getModelState(sessionId);
234:   const modeState = sessionStateService.getModeState(sessionId);
235: 
236:   // Get fossil port for impact buffer links
237:   const runningServer = fossilServerManager.getRunningServer(sessionId);
238:   const fossilPort = runningServer?.port;
239: 
240:   return c.html(
241:     <SessionDetailPage 
242:       session={session}
243:       project={project}
244:       chatHistory={chatHistory}
245:       agent={agent}
246:       modelState={modelState}
247:       modeState={modeState}
248:       fossilPort={fossilPort}
249:     />
250:   );
251: });
252: 
253: // POST /sessions/:id/cancel - Cancel current ACP request
254: router.post("/:id/cancel", async (c: Context) => {
255:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
256:   if (!username) {
257:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
258:   }
259:

265:   }
266:

268:   
269:   return c.json({ success: cancelled });
270: });
271: 
272: // POST /sessions/:id/delete or /projects/:projectId/sessions/:id/delete - Delete session
273: router.post("/:id/delete", async (c: Context) => {
274:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
275:   if (!username) {
276:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
277:   }
278: 
279:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
280:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
281:   
282:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
283:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
284:   }
285:

287:   await sessionRepository.delete(session.projectId, sessionId);
288: 
289:   return c.redirect(`/projects/${session.projectId}/sessions`);
290: });
291: 
292: // GET /sessions/:id/files - Get file tree for a session
293: router.get("/:id/files", async (c: Context) => {
294:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
295:   if (!username) {
296:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
297:   }
298: 
299:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
300:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
301:   
302:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
303:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
304:   }
305: 
306:   // Scan filesystem directly for files
307:   const { readdirSync, statSync } = await import("fs");
308:   const { join, relative } = await import("path");
309:   
310:   const fileTree: { [key: string]: string[] } = {};
311:   
312:   function scanDir(dirPath: string, basePath: string) {
313:     if (!statSync(dirPath, { throwIfNoEntry: false })) {
314:       return;
315:     }
316:     
317:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
318:     
319:     for (const entry of entries) {
320:       const fullPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
321:       const relPath = relative(basePath, fullPath);
322:       
323:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
324:         scanDir(fullPath, basePath);
325:       } else {
326:         const parts = relPath.split("/");
327:         const fileName = parts.pop() || "";
328:         const dir = parts.length > 0 ? parts.join("/") : "(root)";
329:         
330:         if (!fileTree[dir]) {
331:           fileTree[dir] = [];
332:         }
333:         fileTree[dir].push(fileName);
334:       }
335:     }
336:   }
337:   
338:   try {
339:     scanDir(session.agentWorkspacePath, session.agentWorkspacePath);
340:   } catch (error) {
341:     console.error("Error scanning checkout:", error);
342:   }
343: 
344:   // Return HTML file tree
345:   let html = `<!DOCTYPE html>
346: <html>
347: <head><title>File Tree</title></head>
348: <body>
349: <div class="file-tree">
350: `;
351: 
352:   for (const [dir, files] of Object.entries(fileTree)) {
353:     html += `  <div class="dir">${dir}/</div>\n`;
354:     for (const file of files) {
355:       html += `    <div class="file">${file}</div>\n`;
356:     }
357:   }
358: 
359:   html += `</div>
360: </body>
361: </html>`;
362: 
363:   return c.html(html);
364: });
365: 
366: // POST /sessions/:id/chat - Save a chat message
367: router.post("/:id/chat", async (c: Context) => {
368:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
369:   if (!username) {
370:     return c.redirect("/auth/login");
371:   }
372: 
373:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
374:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
375: 
376:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
377:     return c.text("Session not found", 404);
378:   }
379: 
380:   const body = await c.req.parseBody();
381:   const message = body.message as string;
382: 
383:   if (!message) {
384:     return c.text("Message required", 400);
385:   }
386: 
387:   await chatService.saveMessage(sessionId, {
388:     role: "user",
389:     content: message,
390:     timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
391:   });
392: 
393:   return c.json({ success: true });
394: });
395: 
396: // GET /sessions/:id/impact - Get real-time impact metrics for a session
397: router.get("/:id/impact", async (c: Context) => {
398:   const username = await getAuthUsername(c);
399:   if (!username) {
400:     return c.json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, 401);
401:   }
402: 
403:   const sessionId = c.req.param("id");
404:   const session = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
405: 
406:   if (!session || session.owner !== username) {
407:     return c.json({ error: "Session not found" }, 404);
408:   }
409: 
410:   try {
411:     const { impactCalculator } = await import("../impact/calculator.js");
412:     const { getSccService } = await import("../impact/scc-service.js");
413:     const { vcs } = await import("../vcs/index.js");
414: 
415:     // Sync agent-workspace with repo.fossil before calculating impact
416:     const fossilPath = `${session.upstreamPath}/../repo.fossil`;
417:     const { existsSync } = await import("fs");
418:     const { join } = await import("path");
419:     const fslckoutPath = join(session.agentWorkspacePath, ".fslckout");
420:     
421:     if (existsSync(fossilPath)) {
422:       if (!existsSync(fslckoutPath)) {
423:         // Initialize fossil checkout if not exists
424:         console.log(`[impact] Initializing fossil checkout in agent-workspace...`);
425:         await vcs.openFossil(fossilPath, session.agentWorkspacePath);
426:       }
427:       // Sync with repo.fossil to get latest changes from agent
428:       console.log(`[impact] Syncing agent-workspace with repo.fossil...`);
429:       await vcs.fossilUp(session.agentWorkspacePath);
430:     }
431: 
432:     // Check if scc is installed - use getter to avoid TDZ issues
433:     const sccService = getSccService();
434:     const sccInstalled = sccService.isInstalled();
435: 
436:     if (!sccInstalled) {
437:       // Return basic file counts without complexity
438:       const { readdirSync, statSync, readFileSync } = await import("fs");
439:       const { join, relative } = await import("path");
440:       const crypto = await import("crypto");
441: 
442:       const scanDir = (dir: string, baseDir: string, files: Map<string, { checksum: string; size: number }>) => {
443:         if (!statSync(dir, { throwIfNoEntry: false })) return;
444:         const entries = readdirSync(dir, { withFileTypes: true });
445:         for (const entry of entries) {
446:           const fullPath = join(dir, entry.name);
447:           const relPath = relative(baseDir, fullPath);
448:           if (entry.name.startsWith(".")) continue;
449:           if (entry.isDirectory()) {
450:             scanDir(fullPath, baseDir, files);
451:           } else {
452:             const stats = statSync(fullPath);
453:             const content = readFileSync(fullPath);
454:             const checksum = crypto.createHash("md5").update(content).digest("hex");
455:             files.set(relPath, { checksum, size: stats.size });
456:           }
457:         }
458:       };
459: 
460:       const upstreamFiles = new Map<string, { checksum: string; size: number }>();
461:       const workspaceFiles = new Map<string, { checksum: string; size: number }>();
462: 
463:       scanDir(session.upstreamPath, session.upstreamPath, upstreamFiles);
464:       scanDir(session.agentWorkspacePath, session.agentWorkspacePath, workspaceFiles);
465: 
466:       let newCount = 0, changedCount = 0, deletedCount = 0;
467: 
468:       for (const [path, info] of workspaceFiles) {
469:         if (!upstreamFiles.has(path)) newCount++;
470:         else if (upstreamFiles.get(path)?.checksum !== info.checksum) changedCount++;
471:       }
472: 
473:       for (const [path] of upstreamFiles) {
474:         if (!workspaceFiles.has(path)) deletedCount++;
475:       }
476: 
477:       return c.json({
478:         files: { new: newCount, changed: changedCount, deleted: deletedCount },
479:         sccInstalled: false,
480:         warning: "scc not installed - complexity metrics unavailable",
481:       });
482:     }
483: 
484:     // Calculate full impact with complexity
485:     const result = await impactCalculator.calculateImpact(
486:       sessionId,
487:       session.upstreamPath,
488:       session.agentWorkspacePath
489:     );
490: 
491:     return c.json({
492:       ...result,
493:       sccInstalled: true,
494:     });
495:   } catch (error) {
496:     console.error("[impact] Failed to calculate impact:", error);
497:     return c.json({ error: "Failed to calculate impact" }, 500);
498:   }
499: });
500: 
501: export default router;

(End of file - total 501 lines)

101: const server = Bun.serve({
102:   async fetch(req: Request, server: any) {
103:     const url = new URL(req.url);
104:     
105:     // Handle WebSocket upgrade requests
106:     if (req.headers.get("upgrade") === "websocket") {
107:       const type = url.pathname.split('/')[2]; // /ws/agent or /ws/chat
108:       
109:       if (type === 'agent') {
110:         const token = url.searchParams.get("token");
111:         if (!token) {
112:           console.log("[WS] Missing token");
113:           return new Response("Missing token", { status: 400 });
114:         }
115:         
116:         const payload = await agentService.verifyAgentToken(token);
117:         if (!payload) {
118:           console.log("[WS] Invalid token");
119:           return new Response("Invalid token", { status: 401 });
120:         }
121:         
122:         console.log("[WS] Token verified, agentId:", payload.agentId);
123:         
124:         const upgraded = server.upgrade(req, {
125:           data: {
126:             connectionType: 'agent',
127:             agentId: payload.agentId,
128:             url: req.url
129:           }
130:         });
131:         
132:         if (!upgraded) {
133:           console.log("[WS] WebSocket upgrade failed");
134:           return new Response("WebSocket upgrade failed", { status: 500 });
135:         }
136:         console.log("[WS] WebSocket upgraded successfully for agent:", payload.agentId);
137:         return undefined;
138:       }
139:       
140:       if (type === 'chat') {
141:         const sessionId = url.pathname.split('/')[3];
142:         if (!sessionId) {
143:           return new Response("Missing sessionId", { status: 400 });
144:         }
145:         
146:         const upgraded = server.upgrade(req, {
147:           data: {
148:             connectionType: 'chat',
149:             sessionId,
150:             url: req.url
151:           }
152:         });
153:         
154:         if (!upgraded) {
155:           return new Response("WebSocket upgrade failed", { status: 500 });
156:         }
157:         return undefined;
158:       }
159:       
160:       return new Response("Unknown WebSocket endpoint", { status: 404 });
161:     }
162:     
163:     return app.fetch(req);
164:   },
165:   port: PORT,
166:   websocket: {
167:     // WebSocket handler for different connection types
168:     async message(ws, message) {
169:       try {
170:         const data = JSON.parse(message as string);
171:         const connectionType = ws.data?.connectionType;
172:         
173:         switch (connectionType) {
174:           case 'agent':
175:             await handleAgentMessage(ws, data);
176:             break;
177:           case 'chat':
178:             await handleChatMessage(ws, data);
179:             break;
180:           default:
181:             console.log("Unknown connection type");
182:         }
183:       } catch (error) {
184:         console.error("WebSocket message error:", error);
185:       }
186:     },
187:     async open(ws) {
188:       const url = new URL(ws.data.url);
189:       const type = url.pathname.split('/')[2]; // /ws/chat or /ws/agent
190:       
191:       if (type === 'chat') {
192:         // Chat connection
193:         const sessionId = url.pathname.split('/')[3];
194:         ws.data.connectionType = 'chat';
195:         ws.data.sessionId = sessionId;
196:         
197:         // Add to session subscribers
198:         if (!chatSessions.has(sessionId)) {
199:           chatSessions.set(sessionId, new Set());
200:         }
201:         chatSessions.get(sessionId).add(ws);
202:         
203:         // Send chat history
204:         const history = await chatService.loadHistory(sessionId);
205:         ws.send(JSON.stringify({
206:           type: 'history',
207:           messages: history,
208:         }));
209:         
210:         console.log(`Chat client connected to session ${sessionId}`);
211:       } else {
212:         // Agent connection
213:         const token = url.searchParams.get("token");
214:         
215:         if (!token) {
216:           ws.close(1008, "Missing token");
217:           return;
218:         }
219: 
220:         const payload = await agentService.verifyAgentToken(token);
221:         if (!payload) {
222:           ws.close(1008, "Invalid token");
223:           return;
224:         }
225: 
226:         ws.data.connectionType = 'agent';
227:         ws.data.agentId = payload.agentId;
228:         ws.data.authenticated = true;  // Mark as authenticated, waiting for agent_ready
229:         
230:         await agentService.handleAgentConnect(payload.agentId, ws);
231:         console.log(`Agent ${payload.agentId} connected, waiting for agent_ready`);
232:       }
233:     },
234:     async close(ws) {
235:       const connectionType = ws.data?.connectionType;
236:       
237:       if (connectionType === 'chat') {
238:         // Remove from session subscribers
239:         const sessionId = ws.data.sessionId;
240:         if (chatSessions.has(sessionId)) {
241:           chatSessions.get(sessionId).delete(ws);
242:           if (chatSessions.get(sessionId).size === 0) {
243:             chatSessions.delete(sessionId);
244:           }
245:         }
246:         console.log(`Chat client disconnected from session ${sessionId}`);
247:       } else if (connectionType === 'agent') {
248:         const agentId = ws.data.agentId;
249:         if (agentId) {
250:           await agentService.handleAgentDisconnect(agentId);
251:           console.log(`Agent ${agentId} disconnected`);
252: 
253:           // Stop Fossil servers for assigned sessions after grace period
254:           const agent = await agentRepository.findById(agentId);
255:           if (agent && agent.sessionIds && agent.sessionIds.length > 0) {
256:             // 30-second grace period for unexpected disconnects
257:             setTimeout(async () => {
258:               // Check if agent reconnected
259:               if (!agentService.isAgentOnline(agentId)) {
260:                 // Agent didn't reconnect, stop all servers
261:                 for (const sessionId of agent.sessionIds) {
262:                   if (fossilServerManager.isServerRunning(sessionId)) {
263:                     await fossilServerManager.stopServer(sessionId);
264:                     console.log(`Stopped Fossil server for session ${sessionId}`);
265:                   }
266:                 }
267:               }
268:             }, 30000);
269:           }
270:         }
271:       }
272:     },
273:   },
274: });
275: 
276: // Handle agent messages
277: async function handleAgentMessage(ws, data) {
278:   console.log("[agent] Received message:", data.type, data);
279:   process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
280:   
281:   switch (data.type) {
282:     case "ping":
283:       ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: "pong" }));
284:       break;
285:     case "agent_ready":
286:       console.log("[agent] Agent ready:", data.agentId, "workdir:", data.workdir);
287:       process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
288:       
289:       // Store workdir for relative path computation
290:       const agentId = ws.data.agentId;

292:         agentService.handleAgentConnect(agentId, ws, data.workdir);

294:       
295:       // Start Fossil servers for sessions assigned to this agent
296:       // Note: Sessions are assigned via assignedAgentId, not in agent.sessionIds
297:       const sessions = await sessionRepository.findByAssignedAgentId(agentId);
298:       console.log("[agent] Found", sessions.length, "sessions assigned to agent", agentId);
299:       process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
300:       
301:       if (sessions.length > 0) {
302:         const sessionsReady = [];
303:         const workdir = agentService.getAgentWorkdir(agentId);
304:         console.log("[agent] Workdir:", workdir);
305:         process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
306:         
307:         for (const session of sessions) {
308:           const sessionId = session.id;
309:           console.log("[agent] Session:", sessionId, "status:", session.status);
310:           process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
311:           
312:           if (session.status === "active") {
313:             const fossilPath = `${session.upstreamPath}/../repo.fossil`;
314:             console.log("[agent] Starting fossil server for session:", sessionId, "fossil:", fossilPath);
315:             process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
316:             
317:             const result = await fossilServerManager.startServer(sessionId, fossilPath);
318:             console.log("[agent] Fossil server result:", result);
319:             process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
320:             
321:             if ('port' in result) {
322:               // Update session with port
323:               await sessionRepository.update(sessionId, { port: result.port });
324:               
325:               // Get session with credentials
326:               const sessionWithCreds = await sessionRepository.findById(sessionId);
327:               
328:               sessionsReady.push({
329:                 sessionId,
330:                 port: result.port,
331:                 agentWorkspaceUser: sessionWithCreds?.agentWorkspaceUser,
332:                 agentWorkspacePassword: sessionWithCreds?.agentWorkspacePassword,
333:               });
334:             } else {
335:               console.error("[agent] Failed to start fossil server:", result.error);
336:             }
337:           }
338:         }
339:         
340:         // Send session_ready message to agent
341:         if (sessionsReady.length > 0) {
342:           const message = {
343:             type: 'session_ready',
344:             platformUrl: `http://localhost:${PORT}`,
345:             sessions: sessionsReady,
346:           };
347:           console.log("[agent] Sending session_ready:", JSON.stringify(message));
348:           process.stdout?.write?.(""); // Flush stdout
349:           ws.send(JSON.stringify(message));
350:         } else {
351:           console.log("[agent] No sessions ready to send");
352:         }
353:       } else {
354:         console.log("[agent] No sessions assigned to agent");
355:       }
356:       break;
357:     case "thought_start":
358:       {
359:         const startSessionId = data.sessionId;
360:         if (!startSessionId) {
361:           console.log("No sessionId in thought_start");
362:           return;
363:         }
364:         
365:         // Start new thought buffer
366:         thoughtBuffers.set(startSessionId, "");
367:         
368:         // Forward to clients
369:         const subscribers = chatSessions.get(startSessionId);
370:         if (subscribers) {
371:           subscribers.forEach(client => {
372:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
373:               client.send(JSON.stringify({
374:                 type: data.type,
375:                 timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
376:               }));
377:             }
378:           });
379:         }
380:       }
381:       break;
382:       
383:     case "thought_chunk":
384:       {
385:         const chunkSessionId = data.sessionId;
386:         if (!chunkSessionId) {
387:           console.log("No sessionId in thought_chunk");
388:           return;
389:         }
390:         
391:         // Accumulate thought chunks
392:         const currentThoughtBuffer = thoughtBuffers.get(chunkSessionId) || "";
393:         thoughtBuffers.set(chunkSessionId, currentThoughtBuffer + (data.content || ""));
394:         
395:         // Forward to clients
396:         const thoughtChunkSubscribers = chatSessions.get(chunkSessionId);
397:         if (thoughtChunkSubscribers) {
398:           thoughtChunkSubscribers.forEach(client => {
399:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
400:               client.send(JSON.stringify({
401:                 type: data.type,
402:                 content: data.content,
403:                 timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
404:               }));
405:             }
406:           });
407:         }
408:       }
409:       break;
410:       
411:     case "thought_end":
412:       {
413:         const endSessionId = data.sessionId;
414:         if (!endSessionId) {
415:           console.log("No sessionId in thought_end");
416:           return;
417:         }
418:         
419:         // Forward to clients
420:         const endSubscribers = chatSessions.get(endSessionId);
421:         if (endSubscribers) {
422:           endSubscribers.forEach(client => {
423:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
424:               client.send(JSON.stringify({
425:                 type: data.type,
426:                 timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
427:               }));
428:             }
429:           });
430:         }
431:       }
432:       break;
433:       
434:     case "message_chunk":
435:       {
436:         const msgSessionId = data.sessionId;
437:         if (!msgSessionId) {
438:           console.log("No sessionId in message_chunk");
439:           return;
440:         }
441:         
442:         // Accumulate message chunks
443:         const currentBuffer = streamingBuffers.get(msgSessionId) || "";

446:         // Forward to clients
447:         const msgSubscribers = chatSessions.get(msgSessionId);
448:         if (msgSubscribers) {
449:           msgSubscribers.forEach(client => {
450:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
451:               client.send(JSON.stringify({
452:                 type: data.type,
453:                 content: data.content,
454:                 timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
455:               }));
456:             }
457:           });
458:         }
459:       }
460:       break;
461:       
462:     case "usage_update":
463:       {
464:         const usageSessionId = data.sessionId;
465:         if (!usageSessionId) {
466:           console.log("No sessionId in usage_update");
467:           return;
468:         }
469:         
470:         // Get accumulated message and thoughts
471:         const messageContent = streamingBuffers.get(usageSessionId);
472:         const thoughtContent = thoughtBuffers.get(usageSessionId);
473:         
474:         if (messageContent || thoughtContent) {
475:           // Save assistant response with optional thoughts
476:           let fullContent = messageContent || "";
477:           
478:           // Prepend thoughts if present
479:           if (thoughtContent) {
480:             fullContent = `<details><summary>Thought Process</summary>${thoughtContent}</details>\n\n${fullContent}`;
481:             thoughtBuffers.delete(usageSessionId);
482:           }
483:           
484:           await chatService.saveMessage(usageSessionId, {
485:             role: "assistant",
486:             content: fullContent,
487:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
488:           });
489:           
490:           // Clear buffer
491:           streamingBuffers.delete(usageSessionId);
492:         }
493:         
494:         // Forward usage update to clients
495:         const usageSubscribers = chatSessions.get(usageSessionId);
496:         if (usageSubscribers) {
497:           usageSubscribers.forEach(client => {
498:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
499:               client.send(JSON.stringify({
500:                 type: data.type,
501:                 usage: data.usage,
502:                 timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
503:               }));
504:             }
505:           });
506:         }
507:       }
508:       break;
509:     
510:     case "acp_response":
511:       // Legacy: Handle simple ACP response and broadcast to chat
512:       // Agent must specify which session this is for
513:       const sessionId = data.sessionId;
514:       if (!sessionId) {
515:         console.log("No sessionId in acp_response");
516:         return;
517:       }
518:       
519:       // Broadcast to all chat clients in session
520:       const subscribers = chatSessions.get(sessionId);
521:       if (subscribers) {
522:         subscribers.forEach(client => {
523:           if (client.readyState === 1) { // WebSocket.OPEN
524:             client.send(JSON.stringify({
525:               type: 'message',
526:               role: 'assistant',
527:               content: data.content,
528:               timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
529:             }));
530:           }
531:         });
532:       }
533:       
534:       // Save to history
535:       await chatService.saveMessage(sessionId, {
536:         role: 'assistant',
537:         content: data.content,
538:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
539:       });
540:       break;
541:     case "file_changed":
542:       console.log("File changed:", data.files);
543:       
544:       const fileSessionId = data.sessionId;
545:       if (!fileSessionId) {
546:         console.log("No sessionId in file_changed");
547:         return;
548:       }
549:

551:         path: file.path,
552:         isNew: file.isNew,
553:         deleted: file.deleted,
554:       }));

557:       await fileSyncService.handleFileChanges(fileSessionId, changes);
558:       break;
559:     case "session_error":

561:       break;
562:     case "agent_sessions_ready":

564:       break;
565:     case "session_initialized":

567:       if (data.sessionId) {

571:         }
572:         if (data.modeState) {

575:         }
576:         
577:         // Broadcast to chat clients
578:         const initSubscribers = chatSessions.get(data.sessionId);
579:         if (initSubscribers) {
580:           const initMessage: any = {
581:             type: 'session_initialized',
582:             sessionId: data.sessionId,
583:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
584:           };
585:           if (data.modelState) {
586:             initMessage.modelState = data.modelState;
587:           }
588:           if (data.modeState) {
589:             initMessage.modeState = data.modeState;
590:           }
591:

593:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
594:               client.send(JSON.stringify(initMessage));
595:             }
596:           });
597:         }
598:       }
599:       break;
600:     case "model_state":
601:       // Update and broadcast model state
602:       if (data.sessionId && data.modelState) {
603:         sessionStateService.setModelState(data.sessionId, data.modelState);
604:         
605:         const modelSubscribers = chatSessions.get(data.sessionId);
606:         if (modelSubscribers) {
607:           modelSubscribers.forEach((client: WebSocket) => {
608:             if (client.readyState === 1) {
609:               client.send(JSON.stringify({
610:                 type: 'model_state',

612:                 modelState: data.modelState,
613:                 timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
614:               }));
615:             }
616:           });
617:         }
618:       }
619:       break;
620:     case "mode_state":
621:       // Update and broadcast mode state

640:     default:

700:       }

Now I understand the full picture! Let me trace the flow:

**Message Flow:**
1. User sends message via chat WebSocket (`send_message`)
2. Platform saves to chat.jsonl
3. Platform forwards to agent via `user_message` WebSocket message
4. Agent receives `user_message`, spawns ACP process, calls `acpClient.prompt()`
5. ACP process returns streaming responses
6. Agent forwards to platform via `thought_start/chunk/end`, `message_chunk`, `usage_update`
7. Platform saves assistant response to chat.jsonl and broadcasts to chat clients

**So each message spawns a NEW ACP process** (line 394-526 in index.ts).

The current flow:
- `acp_request` message - restarts ACP for a session (line 528-543)
- `cancel_request` message - kills current ACP process
- `user_message` - NOT handled directly... wait

Let me check again - in `handleUserMessage` it just calls `acpClient.prompt()`. But `acpClient.prompt()` requires an initialized session...

Wait, I see the issue now. Looking at `spawnAcpProcess`:

1. Spawns ACP process
2. Creates AcpClient
3. Calls `acpClient.initialize()` which calls `newSession()`
4. Stores in `acpClients` map
5. Process exits after response
6. `acpClients.delete(sessionId)` on process close

So the ACP session exists only for the duration of the prompt! Each prompt = new ACP process = new ACP session.

The ACP session is ephemeral by design - it's tied to the process lifecycle.

So the question changes: **What state is actually lost when the agent restarts?**

1. Chat history: Persisted in chat.jsonl ✓
2. Session config: Persisted in session.yaml ✓


3. Model/mode state: Stored in memory in `sessionStateService` ✗

Model and mode state live in memory (lines 567-575 in index.tsx). When the agent restarts, these values vanish. The agent needs to re-initialize and report `session_initialized` with model/mode state again. This means the platform should persist the last known model/mode state so it can restore it when the agent reconnects, or the agent should query the platform for this state on startup.

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 00:56:25)

Now I understand the complete picture. Let me summarize the key insights:

**The Real Problem:**

1. **ACP sessions are ephemeral** - Each user message spawns a new ACP process/session that lives only for that prompt/response cycle

2. **Model/mode state is in-memory only** in `sessionStateService` - Lost when mimo-platform restarts

3. **When mimo-agent reconnects**, it:
   - Gets `session_ready` message with session info
   - Spawns ACP process → calls `newSession()` → gets fresh ACP session
   - Reports `session_initialized` with model/mode state from ACP
   - Platform stores in `sessionStateService` (memory only)

4. **The gap**: If mimo-platform restarts, `sessionStateService` is empty. When agent reconnects, everything works, but there's a brief period where state is unavailable.

**Current Data Flow:**

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  Current State Persistence                                          │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                      │
│  PERSISTED (survives restart):                                       │
│  ├── chat.jsonl - Full conversation history                       │
│  ├── session.yaml - Session metadata                              │
│  └── agent-workspace/ - File state                                 │
│                                                                      │
│  IN-MEMORY ONLY (lost on restart):                                   │
│  └── sessionStateService - Model/mode state                       │
│      (reconstructed when agent reconnects)                          │
│                                                                      │
│  EPHEMERAL (per ACP session):                                        │
│  └── ACP session context - Lives only during a prompt             │
│      (context window, conversation within that session)            │
│                                                                      │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

So actually... **the system already handles this reasonably well**. When mimo-agent restarts and reconnects:


I see a nuanced challenge with ACP session continuity. The process involves creating a new ACP session, which means the previous context is essentially discarded. While the model and mode states get reloaded, the specific conversation context from the previous session doesn't automatically transfer. This means each restart creates a clean slate for the ACP interaction, potentially losing the immediate context of the previous conversation.

The `loadSession` method might offer a way to restore conversation history, but its implementation would depend on the specific ACP client capabilities. Currently, the system seems to prioritize stateless, independent interactions, which could be both a strength and a limitation depending on the use case.

The core issue remains: how do we maintain conversation continuity across agent restarts, especially when the underlying ACP process is inherently ephemeral?
