So **ACP session resumption is NOT the issue** - ACP sessions are designed to be ephemeral. The real issue is:

**What's Lost on mimo-platform Restart:**
- `sessionStateService` → model/mode state (rebuilt when agent reconnects, but briefly unavailable)

**What's Already Persistent:**
- ✓ `chat.jsonl` - full conversation history
- ✓ `session.yaml` - session metadata
- ✓ Files in workspace

**The Actual Problem to Solve:**

When mimo-agent reconnects after a restart, it needs to know whether to:
1. **Resume normally** - continue with existing session state
2. **Force a reset** - user wants to clear ACP context

And the "Reset Session" you mentioned should:
1. Kill current ACP process (if any)
2. Spawn fresh ACP → `newSession()`  
3. Add system message to `chat.jsonl`: "Session reset at 2026-04-07 15:30:45"
4. Report new `acpSessionId` to platform

**But wait** - since ACP sessions are per-prompt anyway, does "reset" even make sense? The ACP context is already fresh for each message...

Or are you thinking of something else? Like clearing the conversation history (but you said keep it), or resetting model/mode to defaults?

## User (2026-04-07 00:58:41)

we need to store the sessionId from ACP in the mimo-platform, so the next time when mimo-agent is connected mimo-platform will do a 'session/load' using the acpSessionId, is clear?

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 00:58:44)

Ah, I see! The user is clarifying that they DO want ACP session persistence across agent reconnects. So the model is:

1. First time: mimo-agent creates ACP session via `newSession()` → gets `acpSessionId`
2. mimo-agent reports `acpSessionId` to mimo-platform
3. mimo-platform stores `acpSessionId` in session.yaml
4. mimo-agent restarts
5. mimo-agent reconnects to mimo-platform
6. mimo-platform sends stored `acpSessionId` to agent
7. Agent calls `loadSession(acpSessionId)` instead of `newSession()`
8. ACP session is restored with full conversation context

This makes sense if the ACP implementation (opencode) maintains persistent state per session. The user wants to leverage ACP's `loadSession` capability to resume the exact same ACP session.

So the key is:
- Store `acpSessionId` in mimo-platform's session.yaml
- Send it to agent on reconnect
- Agent uses `loadSession()` not `newSession()` when resuming

This is a significant architectural change - the ACP session becomes long-lived across agent restarts.

## Changes Needed

### 1. mimo-platform: Session Repository
Add `acpSessionId` to session.yaml:

```yaml
# session.yaml
id: "sess-platform-456"
name: "Feature X"
acpSessionId: "acp-abc123"  # NEW
```

### 2. mimo-platform: WebSocket Protocol
- On `agent_ready`: send `acpSessionId` if exists
- On `acp_session_created`: receive and store new `acpSessionId`

### 3. mimo-agent: AcpClient
- Support `loadSession()` method (ACP SDK already has it)
- On reconnect: if `acpSessionId` provided, call `loadSession()` instead of `newSession()`

### 4. mimo-agent: Session Lifecycle
- Store `acpSessionId` in SessionInfo
- Report back to platform when new session created

Does this capture it? Want me to create an OpenSpec change to document this design?

  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": 0,
  "result": {
    "protocolVersion": 1,
    "agentCapabilities": {
      "loadSession": true
    }
  }
}
otherwise put a message in the history indicating that the session was resetted

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 01:00:25)

The user is saying that `loadSession` is an optional capability that the ACP agent (opencode) may or may not support. We need to:

1. Check capabilities during initialization
2. If `loadSession` is supported AND we have a persisted `acpSessionId` → use `loadSession()`
3. If NOT supported OR no `acpSessionId` → call `newSession()` and add a system message to history indicating the session was reset

Let me update the flow:
## Agent (2026-04-07 01:00:27)

Ah, perfect catch! `loadSession` is optional per ACP spec. So the flow is:

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  Session Resumption with Capability Check                            │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                      │
│  mimo-agent connects                                                 │
│         ↓                                                            │
│  ACP: initialize()                                                   │
│         ↓                                                            │
│  Check: response.agentCapabilities.loadSession                      │
│         ↓                                                            │
│    ┌────────────────┬────────────────┐                           │
│    │     true         │      false      │                           │
│    │                  │                 │                           │
│    ▼                  ▼                 │                           │
│  Has acpSessionId?  newSession()       │                           │
│    │                  │                 │                           │
│    ▼                  ▼                 │                           │
│  ┌────────┐        ┌────────┐           │                           │
│  │  yes   │        │   no   │           │                           │
│  │        │        │        │           │                           │
│  ▼        │        ▼        │           │                           │
│loadSession│      newSession()          │                           │
│("acp-abc")│        │                    │                           │
│    │      │        │◄───────────────────┘                           │
│    │      │        │                                                │
│    ▼      │        ▼                                                │
│ Success?  │    Add system message:                                  │
│    │      │    "Session reset at 2026-04-07 15:30:45                 │
│    ▼      │    (loadSession not supported)"                          │
│ ┌──────┐  │                                                         │
│ │ yes  │  │                                                         │
│ │      │  │                                                         │
│ ▼      │  │                                                         │
│Report  │  │                                                         │
│success │  │                                                         │
│    │   │  │                                                         │
│    ▼   ▼  ▼                                                         │
│ Report acpSessionId                                                  │
│ to platform                                                         │
│                                                                      │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

## Updated Design

### 1. mimo-platform
- Store `acpSessionId` in session.yaml
- Send `acpSessionId` in `session_ready` message
- On receiving `acp_session_created` with `wasReset: true`, add system message to chat.jsonl

### 2. mimo-agent: AcpClient.initialize()
```typescript
async initialize(cwd, input, output, existingSessionId?: string): Promise<{
  response: NewSessionResponse;
  wasReset: boolean;
  resetReason?: string;
}> {
  // 1. Initialize ACP connection
  // 2. Check capabilities: initResponse.agentCapabilities?.loadSession
  // 3. If loadSession supported AND existingSessionId provided:
  //      → try loadSession()
  //      → if fails: fall back to newSession(), wasReset=true
  // 4. If NOT supported OR no existingSessionId:
  //      → newSession()
  //      → if existingSessionId was provided: wasReset=true
}
```

### 3. Message Protocol Update

**session_ready** (platform → agent):
```json
{
  "type": "session_ready",
  "sessions": [{
    "sessionId": "sess-platform-456",
    "acpSessionId": "acp-abc123",  // may be null
    "port": 8080,
    ...
  }]
}
```

**acp_session_created** (agent → platform):
```json
{
  "type": "acp_session_created",
  "sessionId": "sess-platform-456",
  "acpSessionId": "acp-xyz789",
  "wasReset": true,
  "resetReason": "loadSession not supported by agent"
}
```

Does this capture the full flow including the capability check and fallback behavior?

56:     for (let i = 0; i < args.length; i++) {

59:         config.token = args[++i];
60:       } else if (arg === "--platform" && i + 1 < args.length) {
61:         config.platform = args[++i];
62:       } else if (arg === "--workdir" && i + 1 < args.length) {
63:         config.workDir = args[++i];
64:       }
65:     }
66: 
67:     if (!config.token) {
68:       throw new Error("Missing required argument: --token");
69:     }
70:     if (!config.platform) {
71:       throw new Error("Missing required argument: --platform");
72:     }
73:

76:     }

81:   async start(): Promise<void> {
82:     console.log("[mimo-agent] Starting...");

84:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] WorkDir: ${this.config.workDir}`);

90:   private async connect(): Promise<void> {
91:     const wsUrl = `${this.config.platform}?token=${this.config.token}`;
92: 
93:     return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
94:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Connecting to ${this.config.platform}...`);
95: 
96:       this.ws = new WebSocket(wsUrl);
97: 
98:       this.ws.on("open", () => {
99:         console.log("[mimo-agent] Connected to platform");
100:         this.reconnectAttempts = 0;
101: 
102:         this.send({
103:           type: "agent_ready",
104:           workdir: this.config.workDir,
105:           timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
106:         });
107: 
108:         resolve();
109:       });
110: 
111:       this.ws.on("message", (data: Buffer) => {
112:         try {
113:           const message = JSON.parse(data.toString());
114:           this.handleMessage(message);
115:         } catch (error) {
116:           console.error("[mimo-agent] Failed to parse message:", error);
117:         }
118:       });
119: 
120:       this.ws.on("close", () => {
121:         console.log("[mimo-agent] Disconnected");
122:         this.handleDisconnect();
123:       });
124: 
125:       this.ws.on("error", (error: Error) => {
126:         console.error("[mimo-agent] WebSocket error:", error.message);
127:         reject(error);
128:       });
129: 
130:       setTimeout(() => {
131:         if (this.ws?.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN) {
132:           reject(new Error("Connection timeout"));
133:         }
134:       }, 10000);
135:     });
136:   }
137: 
138:   private handleMessage(message: any): void {
139:     switch (message.type) {
140:       case "ping":
141:         this.send({ type: "pong" });
142:         break;
143: 
144:       case "session_ready":
145:         this.handleSessionReady(message);
146:         break;
147: 
148:       case "acp_request":
149:         this.handleAcpRequest(message);
150:         break;
151: 
152:       case "cancel_request":
153:         this.handleCancelRequest(message);
154:         break;
155: 
156:       case "file_sync_request":
157:         this.handleFileSyncRequest(message);
158:         break;
159: 
160:       case "user_message":
161:         this.handleUserMessage(message);
162:         break;
163: 
164:       case "set_model":
165:         this.handleSetModel(message);
166:         break;
167: 
168:       case "set_mode":
169:         this.handleSetMode(message);
170:         break;
171: 
172:       case "request_state":
173:         this.handleRequestState(message);
174:         break;
175: 
176:       default:
177:         console.log("[mimo-agent] Unknown message type:", message.type);
178:     }
179:   }
180: 
181:   private async handleSessionReady(message: any): Promise<void> {
182:     const { platformUrl, sessions } = message;
183: 
184:     if (!sessions || sessions.length === 0) {
185:       console.log("[mimo-agent] No sessions assigned");
186:       return;
187:     }
188: 
189:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Received ${sessions.length} session(s)`);
190:     const sessionIds: string[] = [];
191: 
192:     for (const session of sessions) {
193:       const { sessionId, port, agentWorkspaceUser, agentWorkspacePassword } = session;
194: 
195:       try {
196:         const checkoutPath = join(this.config.workDir, sessionId);
197:         const platformHost = platformUrl
198:           .replace(/^https?:\/\//, "")
199:           .replace(/\/+$/, "");
200:         const fossilUrl = `http://${platformHost.split(":")[0]}:${port}/`;
201: 
202:         // Setup checkout directory with credentials
203:         await this.setupCheckout(sessionId, checkoutPath, fossilUrl, agentWorkspaceUser, agentWorkspacePassword);
204: 
205:         // Create session with credentials
206:         const sessionInfo = await this.sessionManager.createSession(
207:           sessionId,
208:           fossilUrl,
209:           agentWorkspaceUser,
210:           agentWorkspacePassword
211:         );
212: 
213:         // Spawn ACP process
214:         this.spawnAcpProcess(sessionInfo);
215: 
216:         sessionIds.push(sessionId);
217:         console.log(`[mimo-agent] Session ${sessionId} ready`);
218:       } catch (error) {
219:         console.error(
220:           `[mimo-agent] Failed to setup session ${sessionId}:`,
221:           error
222:         );
223:         this.send({
224:           type: "session_error",
225:           sessionId,
226:           error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
227:           timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
228:         });
229:       }
230:     }
231: 
232:     this.send({
233:       type: "agent_sessions_ready",
234:       sessionIds,
235:       timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
236:     });
237:   }
238: 
239:   private async setupCheckout(
240:     sessionId: string,
241:     checkoutPath: string,
242:     fossilUrl: string,
243:     agentWorkspaceUser?: string,
244:     agentWorkspacePassword?: string
245:   ): Promise<void> {
246:     const repoPath = join(checkoutPath, "..", `${sessionId}.fossil`);
247: 
248:     if (existsSync(repoPath)) {
249:       console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Fossil repo exists, opening`);
250:       if (!existsSync(checkoutPath)) {
251:         mkdirSync(checkoutPath, { recursive: true });
252:       }
253:       try {
254:         execSync(`fossil open ${repoPath}`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
255:       } catch {
256:         // Already open or error, continue
257:       }
258:       // Update remote URL to new port/credentials
259:       if (agentWorkspaceUser && agentWorkspacePassword) {
260:         const url = new URL(fossilUrl);
261:         url.username = agentWorkspaceUser;
262:         url.password = agentWorkspacePassword;
263:         const remoteUrl = url.toString();
264:         console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Updating remote URL to: ${url.protocol}//${url.username}:****@${url.host}/`);
265:         try {
266:           execSync(`fossil remote-url ${remoteUrl}`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
267:         } catch {
268:           // Ignore error, may already be correct
269:         }
270:         // Ensure local password matches server password
271:         try {
272:           execSync(
273:             `fossil user password ${agentWorkspaceUser} ${agentWorkspacePassword}`,
274:             { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
275:           );
276:           console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Updated local user password`);
277:         } catch {
278:           // Ignore error
279:         }
280:         // Update/add named remote "server" with credentials
281:         try {
282:           // Remove existing remote if exists, then add new one
283:           try {
284:             execSync(`fossil remote rm server`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
285:           } catch {
286:             // Remote may not exist, ignore
287:           }
288:           execSync(
289:             `fossil remote add server ${remoteUrl}`,
290:             { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
291:           );
292:           console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Updated remote 'server'`);
293:           // Do a sync using the named remote to verify credentials work
294:           execSync(
295:             `fossil sync server`,
296:             { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
297:           );
298:           console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Verified sync with remote 'server'`);
299:         } catch {
300:           // Ignore error
301:         }
302:       }
303:     } else if (existsSync(join(checkoutPath, ".fossil"))) {
304:       console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Checkout exists, ensuring open`);
305:       try {
306:         execSync(`fossil open`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
307:       } catch {
308:         // Already open or error, continue
309:       }
310:       // Update remote URL to new port/credentials
311:       if (agentWorkspaceUser && agentWorkspacePassword) {
312:         const url = new URL(fossilUrl);
313:         url.username = agentWorkspaceUser;
314:         url.password = agentWorkspacePassword;
315:         const remoteUrl = url.toString();
316:         console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Updating remote URL to: ${url.protocol}//${url.username}:****@${url.host}/`);
317:         try {
318:           execSync(`fossil remote-url ${remoteUrl}`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
319:         } catch {
320:           // Ignore error, may already be correct
321:         }
322:         // Ensure local password matches server password
323:         try {
324:           execSync(
325:             `fossil user password ${agentWorkspaceUser} ${agentWorkspacePassword}`,
326:             { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
327:           );
328:           console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Updated local user password`);
329:         } catch {
330:           // Ignore error
331:         }
332:         // Update/add named remote "server" with credentials
333:         try {
334:           // Remove existing remote if exists, then add new one
335:           try {
336:             execSync(`fossil remote rm server`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
337:           } catch {
338:             // Remote may not exist, ignore
339:           }
340:           execSync(
341:             `fossil remote add server ${remoteUrl}`,
342:             { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
343:           );
344:           console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Updated remote 'server'`);
345:           // Do a sync using the named remote to verify credentials work
346:           execSync(
347:             `fossil sync server`,
348:             { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
349:           );
350:           console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Verified sync with remote 'server'`);
351:         } catch {
352:           // Ignore error
353:         }
354:       }
355:     } else {
356:       console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Cloning from fossil`);
357:       // Use credentials in URL if available
358:       let cloneUrl = fossilUrl;
359:       if (agentWorkspaceUser && agentWorkspacePassword) {
360:         const url = new URL(fossilUrl);
361:         url.username = agentWorkspaceUser;
362:         url.password = agentWorkspacePassword;
363:         cloneUrl = url.toString();
364:         console.log(`[mimo-agent]   Using authenticated URL: ${url.protocol}//${url.username}:****@${url.host}/`);
365:       }
366:       execSync(`fossil clone ${cloneUrl} ${repoPath}`, { stdio: "pipe" });
367:       if (!existsSync(checkoutPath)) {
368:         mkdirSync(checkoutPath, { recursive: true });
369:       }
370:       // Open without sync first, then set remote with credentials
371:       execSync(`fossil open --nosync ${repoPath}`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
372:       // Set remote URL with credentials for future syncs
373:       execSync(`fossil remote-url ${cloneUrl}`, { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" });
374:       // Set local password to match server password (fossil creates local admin with random password)
375:       if (agentWorkspaceUser && agentWorkspacePassword) {
376:         execSync(
377:           `fossil user password ${agentWorkspaceUser} ${agentWorkspacePassword}`,
378:           { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
379:         );
380:         // Add a named remote "server" with credentials embedded
381:         execSync(
382:           `fossil remote add server ${cloneUrl}`,
383:           { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
384:         );
385:         // Do an initial sync using the named remote with credentials
386:         execSync(
387:           `fossil sync server`,
388:           { cwd: checkoutPath, stdio: "pipe" }
389:         );
390:       }
391:     }
392:   }
393: 
394:   private spawnAcpProcess(session: any): void {
395:     const sessionInfo = this.sessionManager.getSession(session.sessionId);
396:     if (!sessionInfo) return;
397: 
398:     // Terminate existing
399:     if (sessionInfo.acpProcess) {
400:       console.log(
401:         `[mimo-agent] Terminating existing ACP for ${session.sessionId}`
402:       );
403:       sessionInfo.acpProcess.kill();
404:     }
405: 
406:     const spawnResult = this.provider.spawn(sessionInfo.checkoutPath);
407:     const process = spawnResult.process;
408:     this.sessionManager.setSessionAcpProcess(session.sessionId, process);
409: 
410:     // Create ACP client
411:     const acpClient = new AcpClient(
412:       this.provider,
413:       session.sessionId,
414:       {
415:         onThoughtStart: (sessionId) => {
416:           this.send({
417:             type: "thought_start",
418:             sessionId,
419:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
420:           });
421:         },
422:         onThoughtChunk: (sessionId, content) => {
423:           this.send({
424:             type: "thought_chunk",
425:             sessionId,
426:             content,
427:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
428:           });
429:         },
430:         onThoughtEnd: (sessionId) => {
431:           this.send({
432:             type: "thought_end",
433:             sessionId,
434:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
435:           });
436:         },
437:         onMessageChunk: (sessionId, content) => {
438:           this.send({
439:             type: "message_chunk",
440:             sessionId,
441:             content,
442:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
443:           });
444:         },
445:         onUsageUpdate: (sessionId, usage) => {
446:           this.send({
447:             type: "usage_update",
448:             sessionId,
449:             usage,
450:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
451:           });
452:         },
453:         onGenericUpdate: (sessionId, content) => {
454:           this.send({
455:             type: "acp_response",
456:             sessionId,
457:             content,
458:             timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
459:           });
460:         },
461:       }
462:     );
463: 
464:     // Initialize ACP client
465:     acpClient
466:       .initialize(
467:         sessionInfo.checkoutPath,
468:         toWebWritable(spawnResult.stdin),
469:         toWebReadable(spawnResult.stdout)
470:       )
471:       .then(() => {
472:         console.log(`[mimo-agent] ACP client ready for ${session.sessionId}`);
473:         this.acpClients.set(session.sessionId, acpClient);
474: 
475:         // Update session state
476:         this.sessionManager.setSessionState(
477:           session.sessionId,
478:           acpClient.modelState,
479:           acpClient.modeState
480:         );
481: 
482:         // Send session initialized
483:         this.send({
484:           type: "session_initialized",
485:           sessionId: session.sessionId,
486:           modelState: acpClient.modelState,
487:           modeState: acpClient.modeState,
488:           timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
489:         });
490:       })
491:       .catch((err) => {
492:         console.error(
493:           `[mimo-agent] ACP init error for ${session.sessionId}:`,
494:           err
495:         );
496:       });
497: 
498:     // Handle process events
499:     process.stderr?.on("data", (data: Buffer) => {
500:       console.error(
501:         `[mimo-agent] ACP stderr (${session.sessionId}):`,
502:         data.toString()
503:       );
504:     });
505: 
506:     process.on("close", (code: number | null) => {
507:       console.log(
508:         `[mimo-agent] ACP exited for ${session.sessionId} with code ${code}`
509:       );
510:       this.acpClients.delete(session.sessionId);
511:       this.sessionManager.setSessionAcpProcess(session.sessionId, null);
512:     });
513: 
514:     process.on("error", (err: Error) => {
515:       console.error(
516:         `[mimo-agent] ACP process error for ${session.sessionId}:`,
517:         err.message
518:       );
519:       this.send({
520:         type: "session_error",
521:         sessionId: session.sessionId,
522:         error: `ACP process error: ${err.message}`,
523:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
524:       });
525:     });
526:   }
527: 
528:   private handleAcpRequest(message: any): void {
529:     const sessionId = message.sessionId;
530:     if (!sessionId) {
531:       console.log("[mimo-agent] No sessionId in acp_request");
532:       return;
533:     }
534: 
535:     const session = this.sessionManager.getSession(sessionId);
536:     if (!session) {
537:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Unknown session ${sessionId}`);
538:       return;
539:     }
540: 
541:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Restarting ACP for session ${sessionId}`);
542:     this.spawnAcpProcess(session);
543:   }
544: 
545:   private handleCancelRequest(message: any): void {
546:     const sessionId = message.sessionId;
547:     if (!sessionId) {
548:       console.log("[mimo-agent] No sessionId in cancel_request");
549:       return;
550:     }
551: 
552:     const session = this.sessionManager.getSession(sessionId);
553:     if (!session) {
554:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Unknown session ${sessionId}`);
555:       return;
556:     }
557: 
558:     if (session.acpProcess) {
559:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Cancelling ACP for ${sessionId}`);
560:       session.acpProcess.kill("SIGTERM");
561:       this.sessionManager.setSessionAcpProcess(sessionId, null);
562:       this.acpClients.delete(sessionId);
563: 
564:       this.send({
565:         type: "acp_cancelled",
566:         sessionId,
567:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
568:       });
569:     }
570:   }
571: 
572:   private handleFileSyncRequest(message: any): void {
573:     const sessionId = message.sessionId;
574:     console.log(
575:       `[mimo-agent] File sync for session ${sessionId || "unknown"}`
576:     );
577:   }
578: 
579:   private handleUserMessage(message: any): void {
580:     const sessionId = message.sessionId;
581:     const content = message.content;
582: 
583:     if (!sessionId) {
584:       console.log("[mimo-agent] No sessionId in user_message");
585:       return;
586:     }
587: 
588:     const acpClient = this.acpClients.get(sessionId);
589:     if (!acpClient) {
590:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] No ACP client for session ${sessionId}`);
591:       this.send({
592:         type: "error_response",
593:         sessionId,
594:         error: `No ACP connection for session: ${sessionId}`,
595:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
596:       });
597:       return;
598:     }
599: 
600:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Sending prompt for session ${sessionId}`);
601:     acpClient
602:       .prompt(content)
603:       .then(() => {
604:         console.log(`[mimo-agent] Prompt completed for ${sessionId}`);
605:       })
606:       .catch((err) => {
607:         console.error(`[mimo-agent] Prompt error:`, err);
608:         this.send({
609:           type: "error_response",
610:           sessionId,
611:           error: `ACP prompt error: ${err.message}`,
612:           timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
613:         });
614:       });
615:   }
616: 
617:   private async handleSetModel(message: any): Promise<void> {
618:     const { sessionId, modelId } = message;
619:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Set model for ${sessionId}: ${modelId}`);
620: 
621:     const acpClient = this.acpClients.get(sessionId);
622:     if (!acpClient) {
623:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] No ACP client for session ${sessionId}`);
624:       return;
625:     }
626: 
627:     try {
628:       await acpClient.setModel(modelId);
629: 
630:       this.send({
631:         type: "model_state",
632:         sessionId,
633:         modelState: acpClient.modelState,
634:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
635:       });
636: 
637:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Model changed to ${modelId}`);
638:     } catch (err: any) {
639:       console.error(`[mimo-agent] Failed to set model:`, err);
640:       this.send({
641:         type: "error_response",
642:         sessionId,
643:         error: `Failed to set model: ${err.message}`,
644:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
645:       });
646:     }
647:   }
648: 
649:   private async handleSetMode(message: any): Promise<void> {
650:     const { sessionId, modeId } = message;
651:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Set mode for ${sessionId}: ${modeId}`);
652: 
653:     const acpClient = this.acpClients.get(sessionId);
654:     if (!acpClient) {
655:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] No ACP client for session ${sessionId}`);
656:       return;
657:     }
658: 
659:     try {
660:       await acpClient.setMode(modeId);
661: 
662:       this.send({
663:         type: "mode_state",
664:         sessionId,
665:         modeState: acpClient.modeState,
666:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
667:       });
668: 
669:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Mode changed to ${modeId}`);
670:     } catch (err: any) {
671:       console.error(`[mimo-agent] Failed to set mode:`, err);
672:       this.send({
673:         type: "error_response",
674:         sessionId,
675:         error: `Failed to set mode: ${err.message}`,
676:         timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
677:       });
678:     }
679:   }
680: 
681:   private handleRequestState(message: any): void {
682:     const { sessionId } = message;
683:     const acpClient = this.acpClients.get(sessionId);
684: 
685:     if (!acpClient) {
686:       console.log(`[mimo-agent] Unknown session ${sessionId} in request_state`);
687:       return;
688:     }
689: 
690:     this.send({
691:       type: "session_initialized",
692:       sessionId,
693:       modelState: acpClient.modelState,
694:       modeState: acpClient.modeState,
695:       timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
696:     });
697: 
698:     console.log(`[mimo-agent] Sent state for session ${sessionId}`);
699:   }
700: 
701:   private handleDisconnect(): void {
702:     if (this.reconnectAttempts < this.maxReconnectAttempts) {
703:       this.reconnectAttempts++;
704:       const delay = this.reconnectDelay * Math.pow(2, this.reconnectAttempts - 1);
705:       console.log(
706:         `[mimo-agent] Reconnecting in ${delay}ms (attempt ${this.reconnectAttempts})...`
707:       );
708: 
709:       setTimeout(() => {
710:         this.connect().catch((error) => {
711:           console.error("[mimo-agent] Reconnect failed:", error.message);
712:         });
713:       }, delay);
714:     } else {
715:       console.error("[mimo-agent] Max reconnect attempts reached");
716:       process.exit(1);
717:     }
718:   }
719: 
720:   private send(message: any): void {
721:     if (this.ws?.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
722:       this.ws.send(JSON.stringify(message));
723:     } else {
724:       console.log("[mimo-agent] WebSocket not connected");
725:     }
726:   }
727: 
728:   private setupShutdownHandlers(): void {
729:     const shutdown = () => {
730:       console.log("[mimo-agent] Shutting down...");
731:       this.sessionManager.terminateAll();
732:       this.ws?.close();
733:       process.exit(0);
734:     };
735: 
736:     process.on("SIGTERM", shutdown);
737:     process.on("SIGINT", shutdown);
738:     process.on("SIGUSR2", shutdown);
739: 
740:     process.on("uncaughtException", (error) => {
741:       console.error("[mimo-agent] Uncaught exception:", error);
742:       shutdown();
743:     });
744:   }
745: }
746: 
747: const agent = new MimoAgent();
748: agent.start().catch((error) => {
749:   console.error("[mimo-agent] Failed to start:", error.message);
750:   process.exit(1);
751: });

(End of file - total 751 lines)

<content>1: import { join } from "path";
2: import { existsSync, mkdirSync, appendFileSync, readFileSync } from "fs";
3: import { getPaths } from "../config/paths.js";
4: 
5: export interface ChatMessage {
6:   role: "user" | "assistant" | "system";
7:   content: string;
8:   timestamp: string;
9:   metadata?: Record<string, unknown>;
10: }
11: 
12: export class ChatService {
13:   private getChatPath(sessionId: string): string {
14:     // Store chat in the session directory
15:     const Paths = getPaths();
16:     const sessionDir = this.findSessionDir(sessionId);
17:     if (!sessionDir) {
18:       throw new Error(`Session ${sessionId} not found`);
19:     }
20:     return join(sessionDir, "chat.jsonl");
21:   }
22: 
23:   private findSessionDir(sessionId: string): string | null {
24:     const Paths = getPaths();
25:     if (!existsSync(Paths.projects)) {
26:       return null;
27:     }
28: 
29:     const { readdirSync } = require("fs");
30:     const projectEntries = readdirSync(Paths.projects, { withFileTypes: true });
31:     
32:     for (const projectEntry of projectEntries) {
33:       if (projectEntry.isDirectory()) {
34:         const sessionsDir = join(Paths.projects, projectEntry.name, "sessions");
35:         if (existsSync(sessionsDir)) {
36:           const sessionDir = join(sessionsDir, sessionId);
37:           if (existsSync(sessionDir)) {
38:             return sessionDir;
39:           }
40:         }
41:       }
42:     }
43: 
44:     return null;
45:   }
46: 
47:   async saveMessage(sessionId: string, message: ChatMessage): Promise<void> {
48:     const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
49:     const line = JSON.stringify(message) + "\n";
50:     appendFileSync(chatPath, line, "utf-8");
51:   }
52: 
53:   async loadHistory(sessionId: string): Promise<ChatMessage[]> {
54:     try {
55:       const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
56:       if (!existsSync(chatPath)) {
57:         return [];
58:       }
59: 
60:       const content = readFileSync(chatPath, "utf-8");
61:       const lines = content.trim().split("\n").filter(line => line);
62:       
63:       return lines.map((line) => JSON.parse(line) as ChatMessage);
64:     } catch {
65:       return [];
66:     }
67:   }
68: 
69:   async appendToHistory(sessionId: string, messages: ChatMessage[]): Promise<void> {
70:     const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
71:     const lines = messages.map((msg) => JSON.stringify(msg)).join("\n") + "\n";
72:     appendFileSync(chatPath, lines, "utf-8");
73:   }
74: 
75:   async clearHistory(sessionId: string): Promise<void> {
76:     const chatPath = this.getChatPath(sessionId);
77:     if (existsSync(chatPath)) {
78:       const { unlinkSync } = require("fs");
79:       unlinkSync(chatPath);
80:     }
81:   }
82: }
83: 
84: export const chatService = new ChatService();

(End of file - total 84 lines)

## User (2026-04-07 01:01:32)

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 01:01:40)

The user confirmed that my understanding is correct. They want:

1. Store `acpSessionId` in mimo-platform (session.yaml)
2. Send it to mimo-agent on `session_ready`
3. mimo-agent checks if ACP supports `loadSession` capability
4. If supported and `acpSessionId` exists → call `loadSession(acpSessionId)`
5. If NOT supported or fails → call `newSession()` and report back with reset indication
6. mimo-platform adds system message to chat.jsonl when session was reset

This is a good design. Now the user wants to move forward. I should ask if they want to create an OpenSpec change for this, or if they want to start implementing.

Since we're in explore mode, I should offer to capture this in an OpenSpec change.
## Agent (2026-04-07 01:01:53)

Perfect! That's a solid design. We have:

**Core Requirements:**
- Persist `acpSessionId` in mimo-platform session.yaml
- Capability-aware session resumption (`loadSession` vs `newSession`)
- Transparent reset notification in chat history

**Key Scenarios Handled:**
1. Agent supports `loadSession` → seamless resumption
2. Agent doesn't support `loadSession` → graceful fallback with user-visible message
3. `loadSession` fails (expired/invalid session ID) → new session with notification
4. First-time connection (no `acpSessionId`) → normal flow

Want me to create an OpenSpec change to capture this design? That would give us:
- `proposal.md` - problem, solution, scope
- `design.md` - detailed architecture, message protocol, capability flow
- `specs/session-acp-persistence/spec.md` - requirements
- `tasks.md` - implementation checklist

I can do `/opsx:ff acp-session-resumption` to fast-forward all artifacts, or `/opsx:new acp-session-resumption` to step through them one by one.

Or if you want to start implementing directly, just say the word and I'll exit explore mode.

Each needs a delta spec file.\n     Use existing spec names from openspec/specs/. Leave empty if no requirement changes. -->\n- `<existing-name>`: <what requirement is changing>\n\n## Impact\n\n<!-- Affected code, APIs, dependencies, systems -->\n",

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/proposal.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 01:04:02
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/proposal.md
content: ## Why

When mimo-agent restarts, the ACP session is lost even though the chat history persists in mimo-platform. This causes the agent to lose conversation context, resulting in disjointed interactions where the AI behaves as if it's starting fresh. We need to connect mimo-platform sessions with ACP sessions so they share the same ID, and enable session resumption after agent restarts.

## What Changes

- Store `acpSessionId` in mimo-platform session.yaml to persist ACP session references
- Extend WebSocket protocol to send `acpSessionId` from platform to agent on reconnection
- Add `acp_session_created` message from agent to report new/updated session IDs
- Implement capability-aware session resumption:
  - Check if ACP agent supports `loadSession` capability during initialization
  - If supported and `acpSessionId` exists: call `loadSession()` to resume conversation
  - If not supported or no session ID: create new session via `newSession()`
- Add transparent reset notification: when session cannot be resumed, append system message to chat history indicating the reset with timestamp

## Capabilities

### New Capabilities
- `session-acp-persistence`: Persist ACP session IDs in mimo-platform and enable session resumption across agent restarts

### Modified Capabilities
- `agent-communication`: Extend WebSocket protocol with `acpSessionId` field in `session_ready` message and new `acp_session_created` message type

## Impact

- **mimo-platform**: Session repository (YAML persistence), WebSocket handlers, chat service
- **mimo-agent**: AcpClient initialization logic, session management, WebSocket message handlers
- **User experience**: Seamless conversation continuity across agent restarts with clear notification when context is reset

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 01:04:19)

The proposal is done, now I need to create the design.md. Let me reference the proposal and create the design document with the technical details we discussed.

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/design.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 01:05:04
**Parameters:**
content: ## Context

Currently, mimo-agent spawns a new ACP process for each user message, creating a fresh ACP session every time. When mimo-agent restarts (crash, redeploy, etc.), any in-memory state is lost. While mimo-platform persists chat history in `chat.jsonl`, the ACP session context (conversation state, model configuration, etc.) is completely reset.

The ACP protocol supports `loadSession()` for resuming existing sessions, but this capability:
1. Is optional (agents advertise it via `agentCapabilities.loadSession`)
2. Requires the client (mimo-agent) to persist the `acpSessionId` returned from `newSession()`

We need a mechanism to:
- Store ACP session IDs in mimo-platform (the source of truth for session state)
- Send the persisted ID to mimo-agent on reconnection
- Handle capability detection and graceful fallback

## Goals / Non-Goals

**Goals:**
- Persist ACP session IDs in mimo-platform session storage
- Enable ACP session resumption when mimo-agent reconnects (if supported)
- Provide transparent session reset notification when resumption is not possible
- Maintain backward compatibility with ACP agents that don't support `loadSession`

**Non-Goals:**
- Changing the fundamental per-message ACP session lifecycle
- Persistent agent-side state (mimo-agent remains stateless)
- Automatic retry logic for failed `loadSession` calls
- Migration of existing sessions (they'll start fresh on next agent connect)

## Decisions

### Decision 1: Platform Owns Session Persistence
**Choice:** Store `acpSessionId` in mimo-platform's session.yaml, not in mimo-agent.

**Rationale:** 
- mimo-platform is the source of truth for session metadata
- mimo-agent is designed to be ephemeral/stateless
- Simplifies agent implementation - just receives the ID on connect

**Alternative:** Agent-side persistence (rejected): Would require agent to manage durable storage, complicating deployment and violating the stateless design.

### Decision 2: Capability-Aware Resumption
**Choice:** Check `agentCapabilities.loadSession` and handle all cases explicitly.

**Rationale:**
- ACP spec marks `loadSession` as optional
- Graceful degradation provides better UX than hard failures
- Clear system messages keep users informed

**Flow:**
```
Agent connects
    ↓
Initialize ACP connection
    ↓
Check capabilities
    ├─ loadSession=true AND acpSessionId exists → try loadSession()
    │   ├─ Success → session resumed
    │   └─ Failure → newSession() + reset notification
    └─ loadSession=false OR no acpSessionId → newSession() + reset notification
```

### Decision 3: Explicit Reset Notification
**Choice:** Append system message to chat.jsonl when session is reset.

**Rationale:**
- Users need visibility into when conversation context changes
- Timestamp provides audit trail
- Distinguishes between "resumed" (seamless) vs "reset" (new context)

**Message Format:**
```json
{
  "role": "system",
  "content": "Session reset at 2026-04-07 15:30:45 (loadSession not supported)",
  "timestamp": "2026-04-07T15:30:45.000Z"
}
```

### Decision 4: Minimal WebSocket Protocol Extension
**Choice:** Add single field to existing `session_ready` message and single new message type `acp_session_created`.

**Rationale:**
- Minimizes changes to existing communication patterns
- `session_ready` already sends session configuration, natural place for acpSessionId
- `acp_session_created` provides clear lifecycle event

## Risks / Trade-offs

| Risk | Likelihood | Impact | Mitigation |
|------|-----------|--------|------------|
| `loadSession` fails silently | Low | Medium | Explicit error handling with fallback to newSession() |
| Stale acpSessionId causes errors | Low | Low | Catch loadSession errors, treat as new session |
| Chat history becomes confusing with resets | Medium | Low | Clear system messages with timestamps |
| ACP agent capabilities change between versions | Low | Low | Check capabilities on every connect, not cached |

**Trade-offs:**
- System messages add noise to chat history, but provide important context
- Additional YAML field increases storage slightly, but negligible impact
- Extra message roundtrip (acp_session_created) adds latency, but only on agent connect

## Migration Plan

**Deployment:**
1. Update mimo-platform to support new WebSocket protocol (backward compatible - acpSessionId is optional)
2. Update mimo-agent to send/receive new message types
3. Deploy mimo-platform
4. Deploy mimo-agent

**Rollback:**
- Remove `acpSessionId` field from session.yaml (optional field, safe to ignore)
- Revert to previous agent version (will receive acpSessionId but ignore it, creating fresh sessions)

**Existing Sessions:**
- Sessions without `acpSessionId` will behave exactly as before (new ACP session each time)
- Field will be populated on first successful agent connection

## Open Questions

None - design is ready for implementation.

filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/design.md

````

Locate the existing requirement in openspec/specs/<capability>/spec.md\n2. Copy the ENTIRE requirement block (from `### Requirement:` through all scenarios)\n3. Paste under `## MODIFIED Requirements` and edit to reflect new behavior\n4. Ensure header text matches exactly (whitespace-insensitive)\n\nCommon pitfall: Using MODIFIED with partial content loses detail at archive time.\nIf adding new concerns without changing existing behavior, use ADDED instead.\n\nExample:\n```\n## ADDED Requirements\n\n### Requirement: User can export data\nThe system SHALL allow users to export their data in CSV format.\n\n#### Scenario: Successful export\n- **WHEN** user clicks \"Export\" button\n- **THEN** system downloads a CSV file with all user data\n\n## REMOVED Requirements\n\n### Requirement: Legacy export\n**Reason**: Replaced by new export system\n**Migration**: Use new export endpoint at /api/v2/export\n```\n\nSpecs should be testable - each scenario is a potential test case.\n",

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/specs/agent-lifecycle/spec.md

**Tool:** read
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 01:05:21
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/specs/agent-lifecycle/spec.md

```
<path>/home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/specs/agent-lifecycle/spec.md</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>1: ## MODIFIED Requirements
2: 
3: ### Requirement: Agent connects successfully
4: The system SHALL allow agent to establish WebSocket connection and receive session information.
5: 
6: #### Scenario: Agent connects with valid token
7: - **WHEN** mimo-agent connects via WebSocket with valid token
8: - **AND** agent sends agent_ready message with {agentId, workdir}
9: - **THEN** system updates agent.yaml status to "online"
10: - **AND** system looks up all sessions assigned to agent
11: - **AND** system starts fossil server for each active session
12: - **AND** system sends session_ready message with {platformUrl, sessions: [{sessionId, port, checkoutPath}]}
13: - **AND** system logs "Agent connected" to console
14: 
15: #### Scenario: Agent connects with multiple sessions
16: - **WHEN** agent connects with 3 assigned sessions
17: - **THEN** system starts 3 fossil servers on ports 8080, 8081, 8082
18: - **AND** system sends session_ready with all 3 sessions
19: - **AND** agent clones all 3 checkouts
20: - **AND** agent spawns 3 ACP processes
21: 
22: #### Scenario: Agent handles session_ready
23: - **WHEN** agent receives session_ready message
24: - **THEN** agent parses each session in sessions array
25: - **AND** agent computes absolute checkout path from relative path and workdir
26: - **AND** agent clones from fossilUrl to checkoutPath for each session
27: - **AND** agent spawns ACP process in each checkoutPath
28: - **AND** agent sends agent_sessions_ready to platform with {sessionIds: [...]}
29: 
30: #### Scenario: Agent connects with no sessions
31: - **WHEN** agent connects with valid token
32: - **AND** agent has no sessions assigned
33: - **THEN** system sends session_ready with empty sessions array
34: - **AND** agent remains connected waiting for session assignment
35: 
36: #### Scenario: Agent reconnects after disconnect
37: - **WHEN** agent disconnects unexpectedly
38: - **AND** agent reconnects within 30 seconds
39: - **THEN** system finds existing fossil servers still running
40: - **AND** system sends session_ready with same sessions
41: - **AND** agent opens existing checkouts (does not re-clone)
42: - **AND** agent spawns new ACP processes
43: 
44: ## ADDED Requirements
45: 
46: ### Requirement: Agent sends workdir on connect
47: The system SHALL receive agent's working directory for relative path computation.
48: 
49: #### Scenario: Agent includes workdir in agent_ready
50: - **WHEN** agent sends agent_ready message
51: - **THEN** message includes workdir field with absolute path
52: - **AND** system stores workdir in agent context
53: - **AND** system uses workdir to compute relative checkout paths

(End of file - total 53 lines)
</content>
```

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 01:05:26)

Now I'll create two spec files:
1. `specs/session-acp-persistence/spec.md` - New capability for ACP session persistence
2. `specs/agent-lifecycle/spec.md` - Delta spec for the modified agent communication capability

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/specs/session-acp-persistence/spec.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 01:05:33
**Parameters:**
content: ## ADDED Requirements

### Requirement: Store ACP session ID in session.yaml
The system SHALL persist the ACP session identifier in the session's YAML configuration file.

#### Scenario: New ACP session created
- **WHEN** mimo-agent successfully creates a new ACP session via newSession()
- **AND** agent sends acp_session_created message to platform
- **THEN** platform stores the acpSessionId in session.yaml
- **AND** the field is named acpSessionId
- **AND** the value is the ACP session identifier string

#### Scenario: ACP session ID is optional
- **WHEN** loading a session from session.yaml
- **AND** the acpSessionId field is missing or null
- **THEN** system treats this as no persisted ACP session
- **AND** agent will create a new ACP session on next connection

### Requirement: Send acpSessionId to agent on session_ready
The system SHALL include the persisted ACP session ID in the session_ready message sent to agents.

#### Scenario: Session with existing acpSessionId
- **WHEN** agent connects and system prepares session_ready message
- **AND** session has acpSessionId: "acp-abc123" in session.yaml
- **THEN** session_ready message includes acpSessionId: "acp-abc123"
- **AND** the field is present in the session object within sessions array

#### Scenario: Session without acpSessionId
- **WHEN** agent connects and system prepares session_ready message
- **AND** session has no acpSessionId (null or missing)
- **THEN** session_ready message includes acpSessionId: null
- **AND** agent will create new ACP session

### Requirement: Receive acp_session_created from agent
The system SHALL accept acp_session_created message from agent and update session.yaml.

#### Scenario: Agent reports new session
- **WHEN** agent sends acp_session_created message
- **AND** message contains {sessionId, acpSessionId, wasReset, resetReason?}
- **THEN** platform updates session.yaml with new acpSessionId
- **AND** if wasReset is true, append system message to chat history

#### Scenario: Agent reports session resumption
- **WHEN** agent sends acp_session_created message
- **AND** wasReset is false
- **THEN** platform updates session.yaml with acpSessionId
- **AND** no system message is added to chat history

### Requirement: Append system message on session reset
The system SHALL append a system message to chat.jsonl when ACP session cannot be resumed.

#### Scenario: Session reset with reason
- **WHEN** agent reports acp_session_created with wasReset: true
- **AND** resetReason is "loadSession not supported"
- **THEN** system appends message to chat.jsonl with role: "system"
- **AND** content includes timestamp and resetReason
- **AND** format is "Session reset at YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS (reason)"

#### Scenario: Session reset without specific reason
- **WHEN** agent reports acp_session_created with wasReset: true
- **AND** no resetReason is provided
- **THEN** system appends message to chat.jsonl with role: "system"
- **AND** content includes timestamp
- **AND** format is "Session reset at YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS"

filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/specs/session-acp-persistence/spec.md

```

## Agent's Thoughts (2026-04-07 01:05:42)

I need to create a delta spec for the agent-lifecycle capability that modifies the existing spec to include the acpSessionId field. Let me read the existing spec again and create the deltaversion.

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/specs/agent-lifecycle/spec.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 01:05:50
**Parameters:**
content: ## MODIFIED Requirements

### Requirement: Agent connects successfully
The system SHALL allow agent to establish WebSocket connection and receive session information including ACP session ID.

#### Scenario: Agent connects with valid token
- **WHEN** mimo-agent connects via WebSocket with valid token
- **AND** agent sends agent_ready message with {agentId, workdir}
- **THEN** system updates agent.yaml status to "online"
- **AND** system looks up all sessions assigned to agent
- **AND** system reads acpSessionId from each session's session.yaml
- **AND** system starts fossil server for each active session
- **AND** system sends session_ready message with {platformUrl, sessions: [{sessionId, port, checkoutPath, acpSessionId}]}
- **AND** system logs "Agent connected" to console

#### Scenario: Agent connects with multiple sessions
- **WHEN** agent connects with 3 assigned sessions
- **THEN** system starts 3 fossil servers on ports 8080, 8081, 8082
- **AND** system sends session_ready with all 3 sessions including acpSessionId for each
- **AND** agent clones all 3 checkouts
- **AND** agent spawns 3 ACP processes

#### Scenario: Agent handles session_ready
- **WHEN** agent receives session_ready message
- **THEN** agent parses each session in sessions array
- **AND** agent extracts acpSessionId from each session object
- **AND** agent computes absolute checkout path from relative path and workdir
- **AND** agent clones from fossilUrl to checkoutPath for each session
- **AND** agent spawns ACP process in each checkoutPath passing acpSessionId
- **AND** agent sends agent_sessions_ready to platform with {sessionIds: [...]}

## ADDED Requirements

### Requirement: Agent reports ACP session creation
The system SHALL receive acp_session_created message from agent after ACP session initialization.

#### Scenario: Agent creates new ACP session
- **WHEN** agent initializes ACP for a session
- **AND** agent either calls newSession() or loadSession()
- **THEN** agent sends acp_session_created to platform
- **AND** message contains {type: "acp_session_created", sessionId, acpSessionId, wasReset}
- **AND** wasReset is true if newSession() was used when loadSession was possible

#### Scenario: Agent reports session resumption
- **WHEN** agent successfully calls loadSession() with existing acpSessionId
- **THEN** agent sends acp_session_created with wasReset: false
- **AND** chat history continues seamlessly without reset notification

### Requirement: Agent handles ACP capability detection
The system SHALL detect ACP agent capabilities and choose appropriate session initialization method.

#### Scenario: ACP supports loadSession
- **WHEN** agent initializes ACP connection
- **AND** ACP initialize response has agentCapabilities.loadSession: true
- **AND** session_ready provided acpSessionId: "acp-abc123"
- **THEN** agent calls connection.loadSession({sessionId: "acp-abc123", cwd, mcpServers})
- **AND** if successful, wasReset is false
- **AND** if fails, agent falls back to newSession() with wasReset: true

#### Scenario: ACP does not support loadSession
- **WHEN** agent initializes ACP connection
- **AND** ACP initialize response has agentCapabilities.loadSession: false or undefined
- **AND** session_ready provided acpSessionId: "acp-abc123"
- **THEN** agent calls connection.newSession({cwd, mcpServers})
- **AND** agent sends acp_session_created with wasReset: true
- **AND** resetReason is "loadSession not supported"

#### Scenario: No persisted session ID
- **WHEN** agent initializes ACP connection
- **AND** session_ready provided acpSessionId: null
- **THEN** agent calls connection.newSession({cwd, mcpServers})
- **AND** agent sends acp_session_created with wasReset: false
- **AND** this is treated as initial session creation, not a reset

filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/specs/agent-lifecycle/spec.md

```

44: - **WHEN** agent sends acp_session_created message
45: - **AND** wasReset is false
46: - **THEN** platform updates session.yaml with acpSessionId
47: - **AND** no system message is added to chat history
48: 
49: ### Requirement: Append system message on session reset
50: The system SHALL append a system message to chat.jsonl when ACP session cannot be resumed.
51: 
52: #### Scenario: Session reset with reason
53: - **WHEN** agent reports acp_session_created with wasReset: true
54: - **AND** resetReason is "loadSession not supported"
55: - **THEN** system appends message to chat.jsonl with role: "system"
56: - **AND** content includes timestamp and resetReason
57: - **AND** format is "Session reset at YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS (reason)"
58: 
59: #### Scenario: Session reset without specific reason
60: - **WHEN** agent reports acp_session_created with wasReset: true
61: - **AND** no resetReason is provided
62: - **THEN** system appends message to chat.jsonl with role: "system"
63: - **AND** content includes timestamp
64: - **AND** format is "Session reset at YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS"

(End of file - total 64 lines)
</content>
```

### Tool Call [completed]: openspec/changes/acp-session-resumption/tasks.md

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-07 01:06:16
**Parameters:**
content: ## 1. mimo-platform: Session Repository

- [ ] 1.1 Add acpSessionId field to Session interface in sessions/repository.ts
- [ ] 1.2 Update session.yaml read/write logic to handle acpSessionId (optional)
- [ ] 1.3 Add acpSessionId parameter to SessionRepository.update() method

## 2. mimo-platform: WebSocket Protocol - Send acpSessionId

- [ ] 2.1 Update session_ready message handler to read acpSessionId from session.yaml
- [ ] 2.2 Include acpSessionId in session objects within session_ready message
- [ ] 2.3 Handle null/missing acpSessionId gracefully (send null)

## 3. mimo-platform: WebSocket Protocol - Receive acp_session_created

- [ ] 3.1 Add handler for acp_session_created message from agent
- [ ] 3.2 Extract sessionId, acpSessionId, wasReset, resetReason from message
- [ ] 3.3 Update session.yaml with new acpSessionId via repository
- [ ] 3.4 If wasReset is true, append system message to chat.jsonl

## 4. mimo-platform: Chat Service - System Messages

- [ ] 4.1 Create function to append system message to chat history
- [ ] 4.2 Format: "Session reset at YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS (reason)"
- [ ] 4.3 Include system message in chat history display

## 5. mimo-agent: AcpClient - Capability Detection

- [ ] 5.1 Check agentCapabilities.loadSession in initialize() response
- [ ] 5.2 Store capabilities in AcpClient instance
- [ ] 5.3 Handle missing capabilities (undefined) as false

## 6. mimo-agent: AcpClient - loadSession Support

- [ ] 6.1 Add loadSession() method to AcpClient
- [ ] 6.2 Call loadSession({sessionId, cwd, mcpServers}) when capability exists and acpSessionId provided
- [ ] 6.3 Handle loadSession errors (fallback to newSession)
- [ ] 6.4 Return result indicating success/failure and session ID

## 7. mimo-agent: AcpClient - Session Initialization Logic

- [ ] 7.1 Modify initialize() to accept optional existingSessionId parameter
- [ ] 7.2 Implement capability-aware logic:
  - If loadSession supported AND existingSessionId: try loadSession first
  - If loadSession fails OR not supported: use newSession
- [ ] 7.3 Return result with {acpSessionId, wasReset, resetReason?}

## 8. mimo-agent: WebSocket Handler - Receive acpSessionId

- [ ] 8.1 Parse acpSessionId from session_ready message
- [ ] 8.2 Store in SessionInfo alongside other session metadata
- [ ] 8.3 Pass acpSessionId to AcpClient.initialize()

## 9. mimo-agent: WebSocket Handler - Send acp_session_created

- [ ] 9.1 After ACP session initialization, send acp_session_created message
- [ ] 9.2 Include sessionId, acpSessionId, wasReset, resetReason (if any)
- [ ] 9.3 Set wasReset=true when newSession used despite having existing ID and loadSession support

## 10. Testing

- [ ] 10.1 Test scenario: Agent with loadSession support resumes session
- [ ] 10.2 Test scenario: Agent without loadSession support creates new session
- [ ] 10.3 Test scenario: Invalid/stale acpSessionId handled gracefully
- [ ] 10.4 Test scenario: System message appears on session reset
- [ ] 10.5 Test backward compatibility: old agent without acp_session_created support
